# math.AT [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Chromatic Euler characteristics and duality for infinite groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28107)
*Gijs Heuts,Irakli Patchkoria*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文研究了一族推广的轨道欧拉示性数（按自然数索引），其中n=0对应经典情形，n≥1对应有限群的色基数。证明了这类广义欧拉示性数可通过Morava E-理论自然解释，并建立了Proper G-等变谱的对偶理论，包括Klein广义Farrell-Tate上同调在T(n)局部系数下的消失性。在大量实例中（包括映射类群和算术群）进行了计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典轨道欧拉示性数（Wall-Serre）和有限群的色基数（Ben-Moshe等人）统一推广到一般自然数指标，并寻求其在Morava E-理论中的解释。

Method: 建立Proper G-等变谱范畴上的新对偶函子，证明无限群G（具有有限proper作用万有空间）的广义上同调具有对偶性，并利用Morava E-理论给出广义欧拉示性数的解释。

Result: 证明了具有有限$\underline{E}G$的无限群G的广义Farrell-Tate上同调在T(n)局部系数下消失；在映射类群（推广Harer-Zagier结果）和算术群（推广Harder结果）等大量例子中完成了计算。

Conclusion: 成功建立了轨道欧拉示性数的一族自然推广，将其与Morava E-理论联系起来，并发展了proper G-等变谱的对偶理论，在多个重要群类中得到了具体计算结果。

Abstract: We study a family of generalizations of the notion of Euler characteristic of discrete groups (or of orbifolds, depending on one's perspective) indexed on the natural numbers. For $n=0$, this is the classical orbifold Euler characteristic as studied by Wall and Serre, whereas for $n \geq 1$ and finite groups, this is the chromatic cardinality as studied by Ben-Moshe--Carmeli--Schlank--Yanovski. For general $n$, we show that our generalized Euler characteristic admits a natural interpretation in terms of the Morava $E$-theories. Our work involves showing that the generalized cohomology of infinite groups $G$ with finite universal space for proper actions $\underline{E}G$ has a good theory of duality, as expressed by a new duality functor on the category of proper $G$-equivariant spectra. In particular, for such groups we prove the vanishing of Klein's generalized Farrell--Tate cohomology with $T(n)$-local coefficients. We compute our generalized orbifold Euler characteristics in a large number of examples. This includes many mapping class groups, where the classical calculation is a result of Harer--Zagier, and many arithmetic groups, whose classical orbifold Euler characteristics were computed by Harder.

</details>

# math.RT [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Representations of infinite species](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27668)
*Raphael Bennett-Tennenhaus,Job Daisie Rock*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了由可能无限个环及双模构成的“种”（species），证明了当每个环都是半单时，其表示范畴是遗传的；利用纯性给出了表示分解为具有局部自同态环的不可分解对象的充分条件；并函子性地构造了带有交换条件的种，生成了来自子对象格、持续同调中的域选择问题以及带缺陷拓扑场论等领域的例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Simson关于种表示的理论推广到无限环的情形，并建立分解定理，同时为来自不同数学领域的例子提供统一的函子性构造框架。

Method: 利用函子范畴刻画表示范畴，证明半单环情形下的遗传性；运用纯性理论（purity）推导分解条件；通过双模值双函子函子性地构造带交换条件的种。

Result: 证明了当所有环半单时表示范畴是遗传的；给出了表示可分解为具有局部自同态环的不可分解对象的充分条件；构造了一族来自子对象格、持续同调、拓扑场论等领域的例子。

Conclusion: 该工作统一并推广了种表示理论，为相关领域提供了新的构造工具和分解条件。

Abstract: We consider species, consisting of a possibly infinite set of rings, and bimodules between them. Simson realised the category of representations as a functor category, which we prove is hereditary when each of the rings is semisimple. We use purity to provide sufficient conditions, in order for a representation to decompose into indecomposables with local endomorphism rings. For any bifunctor valued in bimodules, we functorially construct species equipped with commutativity conditions. This generates examples coming from a range of topics, such as subobject lattices in abelian length categories, the field choice problem in persistent homology, and topological field theories with defects.

</details>


### [3] [The representations of the Lie superalgebra $p(3)$ in characteristic 3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27707)
*Ye Ren*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文分类了特征p=3的代数闭域上秩2的Lie超代数p(3)的所有不可约模，并给出了这些不可约模的特征公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lie超代数p(n)在模表示理论中具有重要地位，但特征p=3时p(3)的不可约模分类尚不完整，本文填补了这一空白。

Method: 利用Lie超代数表示论的标准方法，结合特征p=3的特殊性质，对秩2的p(3)进行不可约模的分类和特征公式推导。

Result: 成功分类了p(3)的所有不可约模，并给出了相应的特征公式。

Conclusion: 本文完成了特征p=3下p(3)的不可约模的完全分类与特征刻画，丰富了Lie超代数模表示理论。

Abstract: Let $g$ be the Lie superalgebra $p(3)$ of rank 2 over an algebraically closed field $K$ of characteristic $p=3$. We classify all irreducible modules of $g$, and give the character formulae for irreducible modules.

</details>


### [4] [The brick chain complexity of an artin algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27879)
*Claus Michael Ringel*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了阿廷代数上有限生成模的砖链复杂度，定义为不可分解模的砖链过滤长度的上确界，并计算了某些代数的砖链复杂度，展示了具有任意大砖链复杂度的代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知任何模都有砖链过滤，本文旨在量化该过滤的复杂度，定义砖链复杂度这一新概念，并探究不同代数的砖链复杂度范围。

Method: 首先定义砖链复杂度：模M的砖链复杂度为存在长度不超过t的砖链过滤的最小t；代数的砖链复杂度为所有不可分解A-模的砖链复杂度的上确界。然后通过具体代数实例计算其砖链复杂度。

Result: 计算了某些代数的砖链复杂度，并证明了存在砖链复杂度可以任意大的代数。

Conclusion: 砖链复杂度是一个有意义的代数不变量，不同代数的砖链复杂度可以差异很大，甚至可以达到任意大。

Abstract: We consider the category of finitely generated modules over an artin algebra $A$. It is known that any module $M$ has a brick chain filtration. We say that M has brick chain complexity at most $t$ provided $M$ has a brick chain filtration of length at most $t$. The brick chain complexity of A is by definition the supremum of the brick chain complexity of the indecomposable $A$-modules. The aim of this note is to calculate the brick chain complexity for some algebras. We will exhibit algebras with arbitrarily large brick chain complexity.

</details>


### [5] [Average divisibility in character tables of $\mathrm{GL}_2(\mathbb{F}_q)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28085)
*Anwesh Ray,Mishty Ray*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限群 $\mathrm{GL}_2(\mathbb{F}_q)$ 的特征表中不被素数 $\ell$ 整除的条目的计数问题，证明了此类条目数量为 $q^4/2 + O_\varepsilon(q^{3+\varepsilon})$，零条目数量同样为 $q^4/2 + O_\varepsilon(q^{3+\varepsilon})$。因此不被 $\ell$ 整除的条目比例趋于 $1/2$，而非零条目中不被 $\ell$ 整除的比例趋于 $1$。这与对称群的情况（几乎所有特征表条目都被任意固定素数整除）显著不同。此外还证明了非零特征值的角度在 $[0,2\pi]$ 上均匀分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受 Peluse 和 Soundararajan 关于对称群特征表的 Miller 猜想工作的启发，研究一般线性群 $\mathrm{GL}_2(\mathbb{F}_q)$ 特征表中条目的 $\ell$ 可除性，以探索不同群族特征表条目可除性行为的差异。

Method: 利用 $\mathrm{GL}_2(\mathbb{F}_q)$ 表示论和特征值理论，通过精确计数和估计特征表中被 $\ell$ 整除的条目数量，结合解析数论方法得到渐近公式。

Result: $N_\ell(q)=q^4/2+O_\varepsilon(q^{3+\varepsilon})$ 对于任意 $\varepsilon>0$；零条目数量同样为 $q^4/2+O_\varepsilon(q^{3+\varepsilon})$；不被 $\ell$ 整除的条目比例趋于 $1/2$，非零条目中不被 $\ell$ 整除的比例趋于 $1$；非零特征值角度在 $[0,2\pi]$ 上均匀分布。

Conclusion: $\mathrm{GL}_2(\mathbb{F}_q)$ 与对称群在特征表条目可除性上表现迥异：前者几乎所有的非零条目都不被固定素数 $\ell$ 整除，而后者几乎所有的条目都被 $\ell$ 整除。此外非零特征值的角度均匀分布，回答了 Miller 关于对称群特征表中非零条目符号分布问题的类比。

Abstract: Let $q$ range over odd prime powers and let $G_q=\mathrm{GL}_2(\mathbb{F}_q)$. Fix a prime number $\ell$. Motivated by work of Peluse and Soundararajan on Miller's conjecture for character tables of symmetric groups, we study the proportion of entries in the character table of $G_q$ which are not divisible by $\ell$, in the sense of divisibility in the ring of algebraic integers. We prove that $N_\ell(q)=\frac{q^4}{2}+O_ε(q^{3+ε})$ for every $ε>0$, where $N_\ell(q)$ denotes the number of entries which are not divisible by $\ell$. We also show that the number of zero entries is $\frac{q^4}{2}+O_ε(q^{3+ε})$. Consequently, the proportion of all entries not divisible by $\ell$ tends to $1/2$, while the proportion of nonzero entries not divisible by $\ell$ tends to $1$. This differs significantly from the symmetric-group case, where almost every character-table entry is divisible by any fixed prime. We also prove an angular equidistribution result for the nonzero character values as $q\to\infty$. We show that the arguments become equidistributed in $[0,2π]$. This proves an analogue of Miller's question on the distribution of signs among the nonzero entries in character tables of symmetric groups.

</details>


### [6] [Stability of the exterior cube $γ$-factors for $\mathrm{GL}(6)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28091)
*Taiwang Deng,Dongming She*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文证明了GL₆上外立方表示的Langlands-Shahidi局部γ-因子的稳定性：对于具有相同中心特征的不可约可允许一般表示，当特征充分分歧时，其γ-因子相等。证明通过E₆型单连通群的最大抛物子群实现外立方表示，并利用部分Bessel积分的渐近展开和高分歧Mellin变换的消失性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立Langlands-Shahidi局部γ-因子在外立方表示下的稳定性，这是Langlands函子性猜想中关键的一致性条件。

Method: 1) 利用E₆型单连通群的最大抛物子群实现外立方表示；2) 显式描述几何商U_M\N'并计算其不变测度；3) 将Shahidi的部分Bessel函数与Levi子群上的部分Bessel积分联系起来；4) 通过部分Bessel积分的渐近展开和高分歧Mellin变换的消失性证明稳定性。

Result: 对于GL₆上具有相同中心特征的不可约可允许一般表示π₁和π₂，以及每个充分分歧的特征χ，有γ(s,π₁⊗χ,∧³,ψ)=γ(s,π₂⊗χ,∧³,ψ)。

Conclusion: 成功证明了外立方表示的Langlands-Shahidi局部γ-因子的稳定性，为Langlands纲领中更一般的函子性猜想提供了重要支撑。

Abstract: We prove the stability of the Langlands-Shahidi local $γ$-factor for the exterior cube representation of $\mathrm{GL}_6$. More precisely, if $π_1$ and $π_2$ are irreducible admissible generic representations of $\mathrm{GL}_6(F)$ with the same central character, then \[ γ(s,π_1\otimesχ,\wedge^3,ψ)= γ(s,π_2\otimesχ,\wedge^3,ψ) \] for every sufficiently ramified character $χ$ of $F^\times$, where $χ$ is regarded as a character of $\mathrm{GL}_6(F)$ through the determinant. The proof uses the realization of the exterior cube representation by the maximal parabolic subgroup of the simply connected group of type $E_6$. We give an explicit description of the relevant geometric quotient $U_M\backslash N'$, compute its invariant measure, and relate Shahidi's partial Bessel functions to partial Bessel integrals on the Levi subgroup. The desired stability then follows from an asymptotic expansion of these partial Bessel integrals and the vanishing of highly ramified Mellin transforms.

</details>


### [7] [On $U(\mathfrak{h})$-free modules of finite rank over $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28096)
*Dimitar Grantcharov,Khoa Nguyen,Kaiming Zhao*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 研究 $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$ 上有限秩的 $U(\mathfrak h)$-自由模（非权模），识别其通过加权函子得到的相干族，描述约当块定义的特殊不可分解模的根滤子，并将结果应用于第一Weyl代数导出的指数模，得到单性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非权模是一类重要的 $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$-模，但对其结构理解尚不充分。本文旨在系统研究有限秩 $U(\mathfrak h)$-自由模这一自然非权模类，并刻画其相干族与约当块结构。

Method: 利用加权函子将 $U(\mathfrak h)$-自由模与相干族建立联系；通过约当块构造特殊不可分解模并递归描述其根滤子；将一般理论应用于第一Weyl代数导出的指数模。

Result: 识别了该模类在加权函子下的像（相干族）；给出了约当块定义模的根滤子递归描述；得到了指数模的单性判据。

Conclusion: 本文建立了 $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$ 上有限秩 $U(\mathfrak h)$-自由模的结构理论，为理解非权模提供了系统框架，并给出了具体指数模的单性条件。

Abstract: We study $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$-modules that are free of finite rank over $U(\mathfrak h)$, where $\mathfrak h$ is a fixed Cartan subalgebra of $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$. These modules form a natural class of non-weight modules. The coherent families obtained from this class via the weighting functor are identified. We also study a distinguished class of indecomposable $U(\mathfrak h)$-free modules defined in terms of Jordan blocks and give a recursive description of their socle filtrations. Finally, we apply the general results to exponential modules arising from the first Weyl algebra and obtain simplicity criteria for these modules.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Massive scalar fields in eccentric regime: Detectability and constraints from LISA observations of extreme mass-ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27429)
*Tieguang Zi,Shailesh Kumar,Jun-Kun Zhao,Bao-Min Gu,Fu-Wen Shu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了围绕克尔黑洞的偏心极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统中，有质量标量场对轨道演化和引力波信号的影响，发现标量辐射可导致显著的引力波相位偏移，且偏心率越大效应越明显；同时利用Fisher信息矩阵分析了LISA对此类标量电荷和标量场质量的测量能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋进（EMRI）是未来空间引力波天文台的重要源，可用于检验基本场存在及广义相对论的偏离。本文旨在研究有质量标量场对偏心EMRI动力学的影响，探索其作为检验标量-张量引力修正的途径。

Method: 在绝热旋进框架下，考虑携带有标量电荷的致密星体同时发射张量引力波和标量辐射，通过频域求解标量扰动方程获得相关相对论性通量，并采用切比雪夫插值实现参数空间内的高效旋进演化。利用相位偏移和波形失配量化标量场质量及标量电荷的影响，并基于Fisher信息矩阵评估LISA的测量能力。

Result: 有质量标量辐射可产生显著的引力波相位偏移，且随轨道偏心率增大而增强；但标量通量随标量场质量增大而受到抑制。偏心EMRI系统能对标量场质量及标量电荷提供有意义的约束。

Conclusion: 偏心EMRI是检验强引力场中标量-张量引力修正的有前景且重要的途径，可为LISA探测标量场提供有效的约束手段。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are among the prime sources for future space-borne gravitational wave (GW) observatories and provide a useful setting for testing the presence of fundamental fields and possible deviations from general relativity (GR) in both strong and weak gravity regimes. In this work, we study the effect of a massive scalar field on eccentric equatorial EMRI dynamics around Kerr black holes. Considering that the inspiralling stellar-mass object carries a scalar charge and emits scalar radiation together with tensor GWs, we compute the relevant relativistic fluxes within the adiabatic treatment of the inspiral. With the solution of the scalar perturbation equation in the frequency domain, the resulting fluxes are presented through the Chebyshev interpolants in order to have the efficient inspiral evolution across the parameter space considered. We quantify the impact of scalar field mass and scalar charge on the orbital evolution and GW signal through phase shifts and waveform mismatches relative to both GR and the massless-scalar scenario. We find that massive scalar radiation can generate significant GW dephasing that increases with orbital eccentricity; however, the scalar flux is suppressed as the scalar field mass is becoming larger. Using a Fisher information matrix (FIM) analysis, we estimate the ability of Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) to measure or constrain the scalar charge and scalar field mass. Our results indicate that eccentric EMRIs can place meaningful constraints on massive scalar fields and provide a promising as well as important avenue for testing scalar-tensor extensions of gravity in the region of a strong gravitational field.

</details>


### [9] [Critical collapse of vacuum spacetimes: Nakamura wave initial data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27431)
*Thomas W. Baumgarte,Carsten Gundlach,David Hilditch*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了轴对称真空引力波在引力坍缩中的临界现象，采用了基于 Nakamura 构造的新初始数据集，该构造将波内容编码在外部曲率而非空间曲率中，简化了非线性约束条件的处理。研究能够比以往更精确地微调数据至黑洞形成阈值，观察到近似自相似解中多一个“回声”，但自相似性并非精确，也未发现唯一临界解的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索轴对称真空引力波坍缩中的临界现象，采用此前未使用过的初始数据集（基于 Nakamura 构造），以提高阈值微调精度并观察自相似解中的更多细节。

Method: 采用 Nakamura 构造，将初始波内容编码在外部曲率而非空间曲率中，基于线性波解构建初始数据并通过“修饰”使其满足非线性约束方程；通过数值模拟对初始数据进行精细调节至黑洞形成阈值。

Result: 新初始数据集允许比以往更精确的阈值微调，观察到近似离散自相似解中多一次“回声”；阈值解呈现近似而非精确的离散自相似性；未发现唯一临界解；不同阈值解的极点与赤道方向出现交替最大值等共同特征。

Conclusion: 研究发现与早期研究一致：存在近似离散自相似的阈值解，但自相似性并非精确；没有证据支持存在唯一临界解；不同阈值解共享一些共同特征（如极点和赤道方向的交替最大值）。

Abstract: We report on numerical simulations of critical phenomena in the collapse of axisymmetric vacuum gravitational waves, adopting families of initial data that, to the best of our knowledge, have not been used in this context before. Like Teukolsky waves, the data are based on linear wave solutions to the Einstein equations. We follow Nakamura's construction and encode the wave content in the extrinsic curvature rather than the spatial curvature, which leads to several simplifications when the data are "dressed up" so that they satisfy the nonlinear constraint equations. We are able to fine-tune these data to the onset of black hole formation slightly better than in our previous simulations, allowing us to observe and examine one more echo in the approximately self-similar threshold solution. Our findings are consistent with earlier studies: while we find threshold solutions that are approximately discretely self-similar, the self-similarity is not exact, and we find no evidence for a unique critical solution. We discuss common features between the different threshold solutions, including the appearance of alternating maxima in the direction of the poles and the equator.

</details>


### [10] [Tidal Forces in the Presence of Torsion and Nonmetricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27433)
*Armin van de Venn,Marcelo Netz-Marzola,David Vasak,Jürgen Struckmeier*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了度规-仿射引力中挠率与非度规性如何修正潮汐加速度，推导了投影偏离方程，并在弱场非相对论极限下分析了相邻自平行线的相对加速度，发现潮汐加速度可分解为牛顿项和由挠率及非度规性诱导的线性后黎曼修正。通过对挠率和非度规性进行不可约洛伦兹分解，识别了潮汐张量中的对应特征，并讨论了未来潮汐测量对后黎曼贡献的约束能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的潮汐加速度理论基于黎曼几何的测地偏离方程，尚未系统考虑度规-仿射引力中挠率和非度规性对潮汐效应的影响。本文旨在建立广义的偏离方程，探索后黎曼几何特征在潮汐信号中的可观测印记。

Method: 在度规-仿射几何框架下推导投影偏离方程，推广标准测地偏离方程；在弱场非相对论极限下对相邻自平行线的相对加速度进行近似；利用不可约洛伦兹分解将挠率和非度规性分解为各分量，识别潮汐张量中的对应特征。

Result: 潮汐加速度在弱场非相对论极限下可分解为标准牛顿项+挠率和非度规性诱导的线性后黎曼修正；通过不可约洛伦兹分解明确了各分量在潮汐张量中的贡献模式；给出了未来潮汐测量转化为后黎曼贡献约束的基准界限。

Conclusion: 潮汐加速度为探测后黎曼时空特征提供了系统性的途径，未来直接的潮汐测量有望约束挠率和非度规性的相关参数。

Abstract: This work investigates how torsion and nonmetricity modify tidal accelerations in metric-affine gravity. We derive a projected deviation equation that generalizes the standard geodesic deviation equation to metric-affine geometry, and apply it to the relative acceleration of neighboring autoparallels in the weak-field, nonrelativistic limit. In this regime, the tidal acceleration separates into the usual Newtonian contribution and linear post-Riemannian corrections sourced by torsion and non-metricity. By decomposing torsion and nonmetricity into their irreducible Lorentz components, we identify the corresponding signatures in the tidal tensor and discuss to what extent these contributions can be distinguished. We then show how future direct tidal measurements could be translated into benchmark bounds on post-Riemannian tidal contributions, assuming probe dynamics sensitive to the affine connection. Our results suggest that the tidal acceleration may provide a systematic route toward probing post-Riemannian spacetime features in the future.

</details>


### [11] [Einstein-aether Elliptic Charges and the First Law of Asymptotically AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27437)

Method: 在静态球对称渐近AdS且c14=0的扇区中，研究人员发现了一种先前未被识别的约化作用量的对称性，由无穷小变换δu^a=f a^a生成（其中a^a为以太加速度，f满足椭圆型约束）。通过推导与该对称性关联的守恒流和荷，并分析对齐极限的物理含义。

Result: 成功推导了与这种新对称性相关联的守恒流和电荷；证明对齐极限自然地对应以太荷贡献为零的系综；建立了爱因斯坦-以太理论中椭圆荷机制的对应物。

Conclusion: 该发现为爱因斯坦-以太理论中Universal Horizons热力学第一定律中额外项提供了对称性解释，澄清了渐近以太对齐的热力学意义，并建立了与Hořava-Lifshitz引力中椭圆荷机制的对应关系。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic role of asymptotic aether alignment for universal horizons in Einstein-aether theory. In the static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically AdS sector with $c_{14}=0$, the known first law for universal horizons contains an additional term whenever the aether is misaligned with the timelike Killing vector at infinity. While this term has recently been interpreted in Hořava--Lifshitz gravity as the contribution of an elliptic charge associated with khronon reparameterizations, no corresponding explanation was available in Einstein-aether theory. We show that, in the same sector, Einstein-aether theory possesses a previously unidentified symmetry of the reduced action, generated by infinitesimal transformations of the form $δu^a=f a^a$, where $a^a$ is the aether acceleration and $f$ obeys an elliptic constraint. We derive the associated current and charge, and show that the aligned limit is naturally interpreted as the ensemble in which this aether-charge contribution vanishes. This provides the Einstein-aether counterpart of the elliptic-charge mechanism in Hořava--Lifshitz gravity and clarifies the thermodynamic significance of asymptotic aether alignment.

### [12] [The crust of dark-matter admixed neutron stars: bulk properties and torsional oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27456)
*Jiayi Zhang,Hector O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了暗物质对中子星外壳及扭转振荡的影响：暗物质会减薄星体外壳（最多12%），并提高振荡频率；该效应与电子屏蔽等微观效应存在简并性，但可通过参数空间区分；扭转振荡有望成为探测中子星内部暗物质核心的观测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质如何影响暗物质-重子混合中子星的外壳结构及其扭转振荡频率，并评估是否可以通过观测扭转振荡来间接探测暗物质的存在。

Method: 构造双流体平衡解（重子物质与暗物质仅通过引力相互作用），采用统一核物质状态方程和费米子暗物质状态方程（含排斥自相互作用），在相对论Cowling近似下推导扭转振荡方程，并对比数值计算与解析公式。

Result: 暗物质使外壳减薄，最大达12%（当暗物质分布在星体内部形成"暗核"时）；振荡频率整体升高，且频移最大的区域对应外壳最薄的区域；暗物质效应与电子屏蔽效应在部分参数空间存在简并，但可被打破。

Conclusion: 扭转振荡有望成为探测大质量中子星内部暗物质核心的有效手段。

Abstract: We study how dark matter (DM) impacts the crust and the spectrum of torsional crust oscillations of dark-matter-admixed neutron stars (DANSs). We construct two-fluid equilibrium solutions wherein baryonic and DM interact gravitationally only, adopting a unified nuclear equation of state for the former and a fermionic equation of state with repulsive self-interaction for the latter. At fixed total gravitational mass and DM mass fraction, we find that DM reduces the crust thickness in comparison to pure baryonic-matter neutron stars (NSs). The thinning of the crust is negligible when most of the DM distribution extends beyond the star's baryonic surface. However, the crust thickness can decrease by as much as 12% when the DM distribution is within the star's baryonic surface, i.e., when the star has a "dark core." We support these results by deriving approximate analytical formulas for the crust thickness that agree with our numerical calculations at the sub-percent level in best case scenarios. Next, we derive the equation that describes crustal torsional modes of DANSs in the relativistic Cowling approximation. We find that the oscillation frequencies are in general higher than those of a comparable pure baryonic-matter NS, with the largest frequency shifts happening in the same parameter space where the crust thickness decreases the most. Moreover, we study the degeneracy between DM and baryonic-crustal microphysics effects on these modes. As an example, we study electron screening, which softens the crust's shear modulus, thus decreasing the frequencies. We find that the degeneracy between the competing effects of DM and electron screening can be broken in some regions of the parameter space we explored. Should they be measured, our results suggest that torsional oscillations could be used to infer the existence of a DM core within massive NSs. (Abridged)

Method: 将暗物质晕建模为各向异性流体，提出满足爱因斯坦场方程精确解的度规形式；通过数值计算和解析推导分析时间与径向度规函数的关系；利用Darmois-Israel连接条件实现内部与外部区域的平滑衔接。

Conclusion: 该工作为黑洞-暗物质晕系统的精确度规建模提供了可行方案，验证了近似反比关系的高精度成立，并为后续研究暗物质对黑洞时空结构的影响奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Following the landmark acquisition of the first image of a black hole, systems comprising a black hole enveloped by a dark matter halo have have attracted considerable attention. This work implements a novel method to analyze the structure of a system composed of a Schwarzschild black hole and a dark matter halo modeled as an anisotropic fluid, while ensuring that the proposed metric constitutes an exact solution of the Einstein field equations. Numerical results show that the connection between the temporal and radial metric functions preserves an inverse relationship, namely $A(r) \approx 1/B(r)$. Furthermore, we analytically demonstrate that the resulting functions satisfy $A(r)B(r) = 1 + \mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$, in excellent agreement with the numerical findings. In addition, the Einstein equations imply that the variation of the product $A(r)B(r)$ is governed by the factor $\varepsilon_h=\frac{8πGρ_0r_0^2}{c^2}$. Finally, we show that the interior Schwarzschild region and the exterior dark matter halo can be joined smoothly via a regular Darmois-Israel junction, without generating any thin-shell curvature steps.

### [14] [Dynamics of Relativistic Binaries in Structured and Stochastic Environments: A Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27526)
*Lorenz Zwick,Conor Dyson,Brian C. Seymour,János Takátsy,Johan Samsing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个通用框架（Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen框架），用于表征引力波驱动下相对论双星系统的非真空扰动。该框架通过滚动平均窗口上的共振谱投影（权重由Hansen系数给出）将平滑、结构化及随机扰动简化为轨道元素的耦合常微分方程组，一致地包含辐射反馳反馈，并能在稀疏时间网格上高效求解。通过变潮汐场中的致密双星和吸积盘中的极端质量比旋进两个天体物理场景展示了应用，旨在统一建模环境效应对偏心及进动双星引力波模板的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波模板大多基于真空近似，忽略了双星所处复杂环境（如潮汐场、吸积盘等）带来的扰动。这些环境效应会在引力波信号中留下特征印记，但缺乏统一的数学框架来系统描述这些扰动如何影响双星的轨道演化及其引力波辐射，特别是对于偏心、进动等非平凡轨道构型。作者旨在填补从唯象模型到真实天体物理环境模型之间的鸿沟。

Method: 1) 将双星运动的扰动分解为共振谱投影，定义在滚动平均窗口上，权重由Hansen系数给出；2) 发展实用判据来识别和评估各类扰动（平滑、结构化、随机）对应的动力学响应；3) 推导出轨道元素的耦合常微分方程组，刻画epi-cyclic、近星点进动和节点进动共振；4) 一致地纳入辐射反馊反馈机制；5) 在粗时间网格上高效数值求解。框架可兼容解析模型和数值模拟输入。

Result: 在两个代表性场景中验证了框架的有效性：1) 变潮汐场中的致密双星系统，展示了框架如何捕捉时变潮汐环境对轨道演化的修正；2) 吸积盘中的极端质量比旋进，证明了框架处理复杂环境扰动的能力。框架在粗时间网格上即能达到高效计算，并一致处理了辐射反馊与共振效应之间的耦合。

Conclusion: 提出Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen框架作为建模双星环境效应的统一工具，特别适用于偏心及进动的引力波源。该框架为构建包含环境效应的引力波模板提供了从物理模型到波形计算的系统路径，填补了唯象模型与真实天体物理环境模拟之间的方法论空白。

Abstract: We develop a general framework to characterize non-vacuum perturbations to relativistic binaries in the gravitational-wave (GW) driven regime, for use in GW parameter estimation studies. The effect of smooth, structured and stochastic perturbations to the binary's motion is reduced to a resonant spectral projection defined on a rolling averaging window, with weights given by Hansen coefficients. This is combined with practical criteria for identifying and evaluating the corresponding dynamical response to perturbations, starting from either analytical models or numerical simulations of binaries in environments. The result is a set of coupled ODEs for the orbital elements that capture epi-cyclic, apsidal and nodal resonances, consistently incorporate feedback from radiation reaction and can be solved efficiently on a coarse time grid. We demonstrate the practical application of the framework in two representative astrophysical scenarios: a compact binary in a variable tidal field and an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral in an accretion disk. We propose the Lagrange-Fourier-Hansen framework as a unified tool for modeling environmental effects in GW templates for eccentric and precessing binary sources, and particularly for bridging the gap between phenomenological prescriptions and realistic models of binaries in environments.

### [15] [Geodesic Focusing Conditions in $f(Q)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27532)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于对称平行几何的测地偏离方程，采用Weyl型非度量性假设，在f(Q)引力中推导修正的Raychaudhuri方程；引入有效能量-动量迹T_eff，将聚焦条件表示为T ≤ T_eff；应用于平坦FLRW背景，分析三种分支下的约束。

Result: 推导出包含物质源贡献的修正Raychaudhuri方程；建立聚焦条件T ≤ T_eff；在对称平行广义相对论极限下，得到三种分支对应的有效迹及对物质内容和连接函数的约束。

Abstract: We study the geodesic deviation equation in symmetric teleparallel geometry (STG), where the relative acceleration is defined with respect to the STG connection. We analyze the modified Raychaudhuri equation along a geodesic congruence in $f(Q)$ gravity under the Weyl-type nonmetricity ansatz. In contrast to the purely geometrical Raychaudhuri equation obtained in general metric-affine settings, the equation derived here contains matter-source contributions through the trace equation of $f(Q)$ gravity. Different from general relativity, focusing in $f(Q)$ gravity is not automatic, and one must impose an appropriate focusing condition. We collect the model-dependent terms in the modified Raychaudhuri equation into an effective energy-momentum trace $T_{\mathrm{eff}}$, so that the focusing condition can be written as the inequality $T\leq T_{\mathrm{eff}}$, where $T$ is the trace of the matter energy-momentum tensor. We also apply this condition to a flat Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker background. The homogeneous and isotropic STG connection admits three branches, each characterized by a single connection function $γ_i$, with $i=1,2,3$. In the symmetric teleparallel equivalent of general relativity, we obtain the corresponding effective traces and derive the resulting constraints on the matter content and the connection functions in each branch.

Method: 提出并实验验证了光反馈控制（optical feedback control）这一新型独立范式，在全尺度引力波探测器上对10.428 kHz的不稳定模式施加光学反馈控制。

Optical feedback offers a novel independent paradigm to mitigate parametric instability. We successfully suppressed an unstable mode at 10.428 kHz, reducing the parametric gain from R = 2 to R < 0.02. ### [17] [Can a regular black hole be observationally distinguished from singular black holes as spinning lens partner in PSR-BH binaries?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27730)
*G. Y. Tuleganova,R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,K. K. Nandi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分析光线到达时间差（TOA）这一新型诊断量，研究自旋透镜（正则黑洞 vs 奇异黑洞）对光信号延迟的影响。结果表明，尽管正则黑洞与奇异黑洞在定性上存在显著差异，但在薄透镜近似下，TOA预测仅在三级或更小量级上表现出差异，因此无法通过观测加以区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在回答标题问题：能否通过光线到达时间差（TOA）来区分正则黑洞与奇异黑洞？作者引入TOA作为一种新型诊断工具，区别于传统的Shapiro时间延迟，用以探测自旋透镜的参考系拖拽效应。

Method: 考虑自旋透镜后方光源同时发出两束光线，分别从透镜两侧绕过到达观测者，计算二者到达时间差（TOA）。以带电正则Ayón-Beato & García黑洞作为自旋透镜，并与Kerr-Newman和Kerr奇异黑洞进行对比，在PSR-BH双星系统背景下做理论分析和数值估算。

Result: 数值估算显示零阶TOA延迟在微秒量级，可被测量。但在薄透镜近似下，正则黑洞与奇异黑洞的TOA预测仅在三级或更高阶小量上存在差异，表明无法通过观测区分二者。

Conclusion: 尽管正则黑洞与奇异黑洞在定性上差异显著，但基于TOA的观测无法在薄透镜近似下区分它们——虽然TOA效应本身是可测量的。

Abstract: To answer the question posed in the title, we consider a novel diagnostic, viz., the difference in the times of arrival (TOA) at the observer of two light rays that simultaneously emanate from a source behind a spinning lens and pass by either side of the lens to reach the observer. This is completely different from the usual Shapiro gravitational time delay, where only one onward light ray is reflected back to the observer. The TOA essentially samples the frame dragging caused by the spinning lens, apart from other lens parameters. Assuming a charged \textit{regular} Ayón-Beato and García black hole as the spinning lens partner in some typical astrophysical PSR-BH binaries, which provide the best laboratory for testing the TOA effect, we theoretically study how the prediction depends on the gyromagnetic ratio $\left(Q/M\right)$ and how it compares with those when the role of spinning lens partner is played by the centrally \textit{singular} Kerr-Newman and Kerr black holes. The numerical estimates for two illustrative binary lens systems show $μ$sec level delay at the zeroth order, which should be measurable. However, the TOA predictions under thin-lens approximation are shown to differ only at third or higher orders of smallness indicating that the regular and singular black holes \textit{cannot} be observationally distinguished despite significant qualitative differences existing among them.

</details>


### [18] [A Lagrangian formulation for Rastall gravity and a covariant formulation for unimodular gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27761)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Rastall引力和unimodular引力提供协变的拉格朗日表述，弥补这些非守恒引力模型缺乏第一性原理推导的不足。

Method: 引入与里奇曲率标量梯度耦合的任意矢量场；分别采用Palatini变分方法和度规变分方法推导场方程；通过施加不同的物理条件约束矢量场，使场方程分别约化为Rastall引力和unimodular引力。

Result: 成功推导了Rastall引力的协变拉格朗日表述；得到了unimodular引力的新拉格朗日表述；阐明了辅助矢量场决定了流形几何是Weyl型还是Riemann型的机制。

Abstract: We propose a Lagrangian formulation for a non-conservative gravity model in which the divergence of the energy-momentum tensor in curved spacetime does not vanish. This is accomplished by introducing an arbitrary vector field that couples with the gradient of the Ricci curvature scalar. We first derive the field equations using the Palatini variational approach. Because the connection and the metric tensor are independent in the Palatini framework, the auxiliary vector field dictates whether the manifold geometry is Weyl or Riemannian. ### [19] [Bounds on the radius of black hole shadows in n-dimensional Einstein gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27795)
*Jiaqi Fu,Yong Song*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了n维静态球对称渐近平坦黑洞阴影半径的模型无关上下界：下界由弱能量条件约束，上界由弱能量条件、强能量条件及渐近衰减条件共同约束，且这些边界被真空Schwarzschild-Tangherlini黑洞饱和，将已知的四维结果推广到任意维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞阴影由最外层不稳定零测地线（光子球）决定，是探测强场引力的直接探针。已有四维模型无关的阴影半径边界，但高维情况尚未建立。本文旨在将这些边界推广到任意维度，为高维黑洞时空的可观测阴影提供模型无关的几何约束。

Method: 针对n维（n≥4）爱因斯坦引力中静态球对称渐近平坦黑洞，假设存在各向异性物质场。下界推导：基于弱能量条件（WEC）证明r_sh ≥ ((n-1)/2)^{1/(n-3)} √((n-1)/(n-3)) r_H。上界推导：在WEC、强能量条件（SEC）及物质场渐近衰减条件下，证明r_sh ≤ √((n-1)/(n-3)) [(n-1)M]^{1/(n-3)}，其中M为ADM质量。

Result: 得到了n维一般黑洞阴影半径的上下界解析表达式，这些结果在四维时退化为已知的四维边界，且被真空Schwarzschild-Tangherlini黑洞精确饱和。

Conclusion: 本文成功将四维黑洞阴影半径的模型无关边界推广到任意维度，为高维黑洞时空的观测阴影提供了普适的几何约束，有助于在更高维引力理论中检验强场引力效应。

Abstract: The dark shadow cast by a black hole, determined by the outermost unstable null circular geodesics (the photon sphere), provides a direct probe of strong-field gravity. In this work, we derive model-independent lower and upper bounds on the shadow radius $r_{\mathrm{sh}}$ for static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat black holes in $n$-dimensional ($n\ge 4$) Einstein gravity, supported by an anisotropic matter field. For the lower bound, assuming the matter satisfies the Weak Energy Condition (WEC), we prove $r_{\mathrm{sh}}\geq \bigl(\frac{n-1}{2}\bigr)^{\frac{1}{n-3}}\sqrt{\frac{n-1}{n-3}}\,r_H$, where $r_H$ is the horizon radius. For the upper bound, under the WEC and the Strong Energy Condition (SEC), together with an asymptotic decay condition on the matter fields, we prove $r_{\mathrm{sh}}\leq\sqrt{\frac{n-1}{n-3}}\bigl[(n-1)M\bigr]^{\frac{1}{n-3}}$, where $M$ is the ADM mass. These results reduce to the known four-dimensional bounds and are saturated by the vacuum Schwarzschild-Tangherlini black hole. Our results generalize the four-dimensional shadow bounds to an arbitrary number of dimensions and provide model-independent geometric constraints on the observable shadow of higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现趋近闵可夫斯基背景时有效"引力温度"发散，强耦合问题被重新表述为热力学奇点；$R^2$ 引力并非恢复为广义相对论，而是无限偏离它。

Conclusion: 热力学类比为 $R^2$ 引力闵可夫斯基极限失效提供了新的物理图像，说明该问题本质上是热力学奇点而非简单的参数极限问题。

We provide a novel interpretation of this phenomenon using the recent thermal analogy between scalar-tensor gravity and Eckart's relativistic dissipative fluids. In this framework, we show that approaching the Minkowski background corresponds to a diverging effective ``gravitational temperature''. This perspective naturally rephrases the strong coupling problem as a thermal singularity, demonstrating that $R^2$ gravity departs infinitely far from General Relativity rather than recovering it.

### [21] [Testing generalized spacetimes for black holes using the Hod function representation of the hoop conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27857)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,G. M. Garipova,R. R. Volotskova,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了Thorne提出的环猜想在正则球对称静态黑洞中的应用。研究表明，仅使用渐近质量$M_{\infty}$可能导致环猜想被违反，而Hod提出的质量函数（Hod函数）可以避免这一问题。作者证明在广义正则黑洞时空中环猜想受到保护，但也指出某些新解存在违反环猜想的问题，从而不能被视为黑洞。此外，作者论证了Hod质量$M(r\leq R)$正是广义相对论中Misner-Sharp几何准局域质量$m(r\leq R)$的物质对应物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证环猜想在广义正则球对称静态黑洞时空中的有效性，并澄清Hod函数与广义相对论中Misner-Sharp准局域质量之间的关系。

Method: 理论分析，通过对广义正则黑洞时空应用Hod提出的质量函数来检验环猜想是否成立。

Result: 环猜想在已有广义正则黑洞时空中受到保护；但某些新提出的解会违反环猜想，不支持其作为黑洞；Hod质量是Misner-Sharp几何准局域质量的物质对应。

Conclusion: 环猜想通过Hod函数在正则黑洞中得以维持，但并非所有解都能满足该猜想；Hod函数本质上就是广义相对论中的几何量，因此基于Hod函数的结论等同于广义相对论的结论。

Abstract: The hoop conjecture, due to Thorne, is a fundamental aspect of black holes in classical general relativity. Recently, generalized classes of regular spherically symmetric static black holes with arbitrary exponents coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics have been constructed in the literature. The conjecture in those spacetimes could be violated if only the asymptotic mass $M_{\infty}$ is used. To avoid such violations, Hod earlier suggested the appropriate mass function and stated the conjecture in terms of what we call the Hod function. The conjecture can then be applied to any given static spacetime to test whether or not it represents black holes. It is shown here that the conjecture is protected in the above constructed class of generalized spacetimes thus supporting them as black holes. However, it is argued that there are factors, including violation of the conjecture, that militate against the proposed \textit{new} class of solutions to be qualifying as black holes. Finally, we exemplify that the Hod mass $M(r\leq R)$ in the conjecture is exactly the \textit{matter} counterpart of the Misner-Sharp \textit{geometrical} quasilocal mass $m(r\leq R)$ of general relativity. Thus any conclusion based on Hod function is strictly a conclusion of general relativity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 建立了Kerr黑洞内视界附近量子场的完整渐近图像：环降加逆幂律尾的衰减模式，环降频率与经典准正则模的关系，以及普适的Price律类似行为。

Abstract: We compute $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ as well as the energy fluxes $\langle \hat{T}_{uu}\rangle_\text{ren}$ and $\langle \hat{T}_{vv}\rangle_\text{ren}$ (where $u$ and $v$ are the standard Eddington-Finkelstein coordinates) associated with a quantum massless real scalar field $\hatΦ$, with a general curvature coupling constant $ξ$, near the inner horizon (IH) of a Kerr black hole, along the axis of rotation. The quantum field is in the Unruh state, corresponding to an evaporating black hole. We renormalize these quantities by the state-subtraction method. We drop the assumption of minimal coupling to the curvature, thereby generalizing the results of arXiv:2203.08502 for the fluxes at the IH. This requires understanding the asymptotic behavior of $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ neat the IH. State subtraction allows us to push the computation of $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ along the axis of rotation in the Kerr interior in arXiv:2409.17464 deeper into the near-IH region, exposing their final asymptotic behavior on approaching the IH. For $\langle\hatΦ^{2}\rangle_\text{ren}$ (a $ξ$-independent quantity in the Kerr case), we find that the approach to its finite asymptotic IH value is given, per $\ell$-mode, by a ringdown phase (namely exponentially damped oscillations), followed by an inverse-power tail, both in the tortoise coordinate $r_{*}$ (which diverges at the IH). Interestingly, in the regime where the ringing dominates, the ringing's complex frequencies are (numerically) found to match twice the well-known classical quasinormal-mode frequencies in Kerr, and the inverse-power tails are found to be $r_{*}^{-2\ell-3}$ (resembling Price's law in the classical black hole exterior, upon replacement $t\to r_*$). ### [23] [Comparing accretion disk profiles of Bogush-Galt'sov naked singularity and Kerr black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27877)

Method: 采用Novikov-Thorne薄吸积盘模型，对Bogush和Gal'tsov最新报道的带有标量荷σ的自旋裸奇点进行吸积特性分析，并与Kerr黑洞进行定量比较。

Abstract: It is well known that the Einstein-scalar system of general relativity can in principle yield non-unique exact spinning naked singularities, which lead to unique Kerr black hole when the scalar field is switched off. It is a challenging task to observationally distinguish these two types of objects. Since accretion process could be a viable diagnostic for this distinction, the purpose of the present work is to explore whether there could be features in the accretion profiles distinguishing the singularity from a Kerr black hole. Here we study the Novikov-Thorne thin accretion to a \textit{new} spinning naked singularity with a scalar charge $σ$ recently reported by Bogush and Gal'tsov (BG). Our study reveals that: (1) The conversion efficiency $ε$ of the BG naked singularity is \textit{independent} of $σ$ and (2) The maxima of emissivity profiles for the BG singularity tend to shift towards the inner disk ISCO boundary $r=r_{ms}$ and peak at a value significantly larger than those of a Kerr black hole with the increase of $a$, $σ$ and relative shrinking of $\sqrt{-g}$. All these effects are \textit{quantitatively} tabulated, which reveal, for instance, that the flux from the naked singularity could be as high as $10^{5}$ times larger than that of a Kerr black hole. Since these distinguishing features are known to be shared also by other models of naked singularity, it is tempting to speculate that such behavior could be hallmark of naked singularities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of a charged massive scalar field around Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson Black Holes. We demonstrate that within a specific frequency band, the external magnetic field alters the physical boundary condition at the horizon from a propagating state to a purely exponentially decaying state, strictly locking the dissipation to zero ($\text{Im}(ω) = 0$). Consequently, the system supports two physically distinct classes of stationary bound states. Alongside the classical synchronized scalar clouds (Type-I) existing strictly at the superradiant threshold, we identify a new class of scalar clouds that exponentially decay at the event horizon (Type-II). Supported by precise numerical integrations, we demonstrate the spatial structure of these configurations. Our findings reveal that magnetized astrophysical environments can harbor significantly richer bosonic configurations than standard isolated black holes.

Method: 在六维膜世界（2DD）框架下计算高维PBH的演化，引入记忆负担效应（记忆指数p=2）；利用四维形式论计算标量诱导的次级引力波背景；使用Fisher预测分析约束PBH质量、暗物质占比和原初曲率谱宽度。

Abstract: We study primordial-black-hole (PBH) dark matter in the two-dark-dimensions (2DD) framework, a six-dimensional brane-world scenario with two compact extra dimensions and a fundamental gravity scale of order $10\,\mathrm{TeV}$. We calculate the evolution of higher-dimensional PBHs including the recently proposed quantum-gravitational memory-burden effect. For a memory exponent $p=2$, the evaporation rate is strongly suppressed, allowing PBHs with initial masses as small as $\sim10^{-3}\,\mathrm{g}$ to survive until the present epoch. Consequently, PBHs can account for the observed dark matter over a mass range extending from $10^{-3}\,\mathrm{g}$ to $10^{21}\,\mathrm{g}$. We further compute the stochastic gravitational-wave background generated at second order by the primordial curvature perturbations responsible for PBH formation. We show that the conventional four-dimensional formalism for scalar-induced gravitational waves remains applicable throughout the mass range accessible to current and future gravitational wave experiments. The resulting signals can be probed by LISA, DECIGO, and pulsar timing arrays. Using Fisher forecasts, we find that these observations can constrain the PBH mass, dark-matter fraction, and width of the primordial curvature spectrum with high precision. The low fundamental gravity scale of the 2DD framework also permits the production of microscopic black holes at future high-energy colliders. Their decay signatures, together with gravitational-wave measurements, provide complementary tests of higher-dimensional gravity, the memory-burden mechanism, and primordial-black-hole dark matter.

### [26] [Revisit Static Aether: Exact Vacuum Solution in Einstein-Aether Theory and Its Analytic Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27995)
*Jie Zhu,Hao Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-以太理论中获得了严格静态以太构型的精确解析真空解，并研究了其最大延拓。该解仅依赖于耦合参数$c_{14}$，在$c_{14}=0$极限下退化为史瓦西几何。研究表明史瓦西解是该族解的孤立成员：任何非零$c_{14}$都会使时空不再是黑洞，而是变成裸奇点（$c_{14}<0$）或类虫洞几何（$0<c_{14}<2$）。通过构建完全解析延拓，揭示了虫洞的内部无穷远对应于极值 Killing 视界，穿越该视界进入新时空区域，其中时间与径向坐标的因果角色互换，时空最终终止于类空奇点。相应的卡特-彭罗斯图展示了静态以太真空时空先前未被探索的因果完备化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索爱因斯坦-以太理论中静态以太构型下的精确解析真空解及其全局因果结构，特别是非零耦合参数$c_{14}$如何改变时空几何的黑洞性质，填补该理论中真空解最大延拓与因果结构研究的空白。

Method: 1. 在爱因斯坦-以太理论框架下，假设严格静态以太构型，推导出依赖于耦合参数$c_{14}$的精确解析真空解。2. 对解进行解析延拓，构建完整的时空扩展。3. 通过分析Killing视界、因果结构及奇点性质，绘制卡特-彭罗斯图总结全局结构。

Result: 1. 获得了仅依赖于$c_{14}$的精确静态真空解，在$c_{14}=0$时退化为史瓦西解。2. 史瓦西解是该族解的孤立成员：$c_{14}<0$时为裸奇点；$0<c_{14}<2$时为类虫洞几何。3. 虫洞内部无穷远对应极值Killing视界，穿越后时间与径向坐标因果角色互换，时空最终终止于类空奇点。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦-以太理论中的静态真空解在非零耦合参数下与广义相对论的史瓦西解存在本质差异，揭示了该理论中全新的因果完备化结构，对理解修改引力理论中时空拓扑和因果结构具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: We obtain an exact analytical vacuum solution of Einstein-Aether theory with a strictly static aether configuration and investigate its maximal extension. The solution depends only on the coupling $c_{14}$ and reduces to the Schwarzschild geometry in the limit $c_{14}=0$. We show that Schwarzschild is an isolated member of this family: for any nonzero $c_{14}$ the spacetime ceases to be a black hole and instead becomes either a naked singularity ($c_{14}<0$) or a wormhole-like geometry ($0<c_{14}<2$). By constructing the complete analytic extension, we demonstrate that the internal infinity of the wormhole corresponds to an extremal Killing horizon. Crossing this horizon leads to a new spacetime region where the causal roles of time and radial coordinates are exchanged, and the spacetime ultimately terminates at a spacelike singularity. The resulting global structure, summarized by the corresponding Carter-Penrose diagrams, reveals a previously unexplored causal completion of the static-aether vacuum spacetime.

</details>


### [27] [Construction of Sensitivity Curves for Dynamic LISA and Taiji](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28071)
*Hong-Yu Shi,Yong Tang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了LISA和天琴等天基引力波激光干涉仪在一年日心轨道上的方向依赖响应和灵敏度，发现动态模型相比静态近似在低频灵敏度上存在约20%的差异，导致可探测引力波源数量的方向依赖性变化约70%，因此需要采用全动态、方向依赖的灵敏度曲线进行准确预测和参数推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LISA类探测器常被建模为静态等边三角形星座，该近似忽略了轨道运动和方向依赖性，而灵敏度和响应对科学目标、任务设计和参数估计至关重要，因此需要系统研究动态探测器真实的方向依赖响应。

Method: 基于解析的时变日心轨道模型和绝热不等臂干涉仪配置，在Michelson干涉通道中构建了动态LISA和天琴的方向依赖灵敏度曲线，并推导了角度依赖灵敏度的解析表达式。

Result: 低频灵敏度相对于静态近似变化约20%，可探测引力波源数量的方向依赖性变化约70%，高频差异更大；在低频天图中出现象限状图案。

Conclusion: 准确预测引力波源总数和可靠推断双星系统参数必须采用全动态、方向依赖的灵敏度曲线，静态近似不足以满足精度要求。

Abstract: Space-based gravitational-wave (GW) laser interferometers, including LISA and Taiji, are designed to observe gravitational waves in the millihertz band and are expected to open up a frequency range that is otherwise inaccessible. The sensitivity and response of these instruments are central to their scientific goals, mission design and parameter estimation capabilities. However, they are commonly modeled as static, equilateral triangular constellations, an approximation that neglects both orbital motion and directional dependence. In this work, we systematically examine the direction-dependent response and sensitivity of dynamic LISA-like detectors over an entire year of heliocentric orbit. Based on an analytical, time-dependent heliocentric orbital model and an adiabatic unequal-arm interferometer configuration, we construct direction-dependent sensitivity curves in the Michelson interferometric channel for dynamic LISA and Taiji. We obtain analytic expressions for the angular-dependent sensitivity and demonstrate the emergence of a quadrant-like pattern in sky maps at low frequencies. We show that, relative to the static approximation, the low-frequency sensitivity varies by roughly $20\%$, which in turn produces about a $70\%$ variation in the directional dependence of the number of detectable GW sources, with even larger discrepancies at higher frequencies. Therefore, for accurate predictions of the total GW source counts and reliable parameter inference for binary systems, it is necessary to employ fully dynamic, direction-dependent sensitivity curves.

### [28] [Joint inference of line-of-sight acceleration and orbital eccentricity in neutron-star--black-hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28156)
*Lorenzo Pompili,Aldo Gamboa,Alessandra Buonanno*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在时域上对引力波应变进行重映射以实现视线加速度（LOSA）修正的方法，该方法统一适用于高阶模式、自旋进动和轨道偏心率，并将其部署在SEOBNRv6EHM和SEOBNRv5PHM模型中。通过对五个NSBH事件的联合推断，发现所有事件均与零LOSA一致，但GW200105_162426的联合后验倾向于不支持Γ和e同时为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密双星系统的视线加速度（LOSA）可提供动力学形成环境的单事件诊断，但波形建模的系统误差（缺失高阶模式、自旋进动或轨道偏心率）可能模仿或掩盖非零LOSA信号，因此波形精度是LOSA推断的关键问题。

Method: 在时域上对引力波应变进行重映射来实现LOSA修正，该方法统一适用于所有模式内容、自旋进动和轨道偏心率，并自然集成到包含这些效应的时域旋进-并合-衰荡模型中。具体部署在SEOBNRv6EHM（对准自旋偏心模型）和SEOBNRv5PHM（进动准圆形模型）中。

Result: SEOBNRv6EHM能正确恢复偏心信号和自旋进动注入信号中的LOSA，而SEOBNRv5PHM在偏心信号上会产生虚假的LOSA测量。对五个NSBH事件的联合推断显示所有事件均与零LOSA一致，但GW200105_162426的联合后验在90%置信度下不支持Γ和e同时为零。

Conclusion: 研究验证了时域LOSA修正方法的有效性，发现模型选择对偏心信号的LOSA推断至关重要。对LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA目录中五个NSBH事件的首次LOSA约束表明，GW200105_162426的联合后验支持了先前分析中关于偏心率的提示。

Abstract: A line-of-sight acceleration (LOSA) of a compact-binary center of mass, imparted for example by a nearby tertiary perturber, imprints a Doppler modulation on the gravitational-wave signal and provides a single-event diagnostic of dynamical formation environments. Waveform-modeling systematics -- missing higher-order modes, spin precession, or orbital eccentricity -- can mimic or mask a non-zero LOSA, making waveform accuracy a leading concern for LOSA inference. We implement LOSA corrections directly in the time domain as a remap of the strain: the treatment applies uniformly to all mode content, spin precession, and orbital eccentricity, and integrates naturally with time-domain inspiral-merger-ringdown models that best capture these effects. We deploy it in the SEOBNRv6EHM (aligned-spin eccentric) and SEOBNRv5PHM (precessing quasi-circular) models, and validate the implementation on simulated signals; we find that SEOBNRv6EHM recovers LOSA correctly on both eccentric and spin-precessing injections, while SEOBNRv5PHM yields a spurious LOSA measurement on eccentric signals. Motivated by the eccentricity hints in the neutron-star--black-hole (NSBH) event GW200105_162426 and the favorable low-mass regime of these sources, we jointly infer LOSA and orbital eccentricity for the five NSBH events in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA catalog, reporting the first LOSA constraints on three of them. All five events are consistent with a vanishing LOSA, $Γ\equiv a_\parallel/c = 0$; for GW200105_162426, the joint $(Γ, e)$ posterior nonetheless disfavors both $Γ$ and $e$ being zero simultaneously at 90% credibility, supporting the eccentricity hints reported in previous analyses.

### [29] [Finite Coherence in Gravitational Waves from Tidally Excited Axion Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28161)
*Yizhi Liang,Mian Zhu,Wen-Biao Han,Lianfu Wei,Peng Wang,Jun Tao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索旋转黑洞周围轴子云（引力原子）在双星系统中的潮汐跃迁所辐射的引力波信号，特别是强耦合玻尔交叉情况下的相干性效应，以提供对轴子云动力学的引力波探测手段。

Method: 通过分析二能级相干性在潮汐跃迁中的作用，研究不同扫描速率下（绝热、中间、弱通过）的跃迁波形和轨道响应，并考虑大质量系统中的精细和超精细跃迁效应。

Result: 发现相干性在绝热分支和弱通过极限下被抑制，但在中间扫描速率下存活并产生有限跃迁波形；大质量系统中精细/超精细跃迁产生窄带引力辐射及累积的波形偏差。

Conclusion: 相干潮汐交叉可作为引力波探测轴子云动力学的有效探针，为观测黑洞超辐射现象提供新途径。

Abstract: Axion clouds around rotating black holes form gravitational atoms whose tidal transitions can radiate gravitational waves in binaries. For strongly coupled Bohr crossings, transition radiation is governed by the outgoing two-level coherence, not by the transition probability alone. This coherence is suppressed both on the adiabatic branch and in the weak passage limit, but survives for intermediate sweep rates, producing a finite transition waveform and a localized orbital response. In more massive systems, fine and hyperfine transitions produce narrowband gravitational radiation and cumulative departures from vacuum binary waveforms. Coherent tidal crossings offer a gravitational-wave probe of axion-cloud dynamics.

### [30] [Gravitational-wave response functions for space-borne detectors based on multiple geometric time-delay interferometry links](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28173)
*Rui Luo,Pan-Pan Wang,Lin-Lin Yang,Xin-Lei Zhao,Cheng-Gang Shao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天基引力波探测的主要挑战是从远大于信号水平的仪器噪声中提取微弱的引力波信号。TDI技术虽能抑制主导的激光相位噪声，但现有的TDI组合响应函数推导方法较为繁琐，缺乏统一的公式化框架，导致计算复杂度高且物理意义不够清晰。

Method: 将激光多普勒频移的表示从单一探测臂扩展到多种几何构型（如往返链和非往返链），基于此提出广义的链路映射规则，并重新推导了45种第二代TDI组合的响应函数。

Result: 新的公式化方法显著精简了多种TDI组合的数学表达式，增强了物理清晰度；链路映射规则能高效构建这些TDI组合的响应函数，并降低了计算复杂度。

Conclusion: 该广义方法为未来天基引力波任务的数据处理提供了可靠的理论与算法基础，具有重要的工程应用价值。

Abstract: The primary challenge for space-borne gravitational wave (GW) detectors lies in extracting the weak GW signal from instrumental noise that exceeds the signal level by many orders of magnitude. Time-delay interferometry (TDI) addresses this by suppressing the dominant laser phase noise through recombination of time-delayed measurement data. The detector's response to a GW signal is represented in the frequency domain by a response function. Currently, the GW signal response is first expressed in terms of the Doppler frequency shift in a single detection arm, and this formulation is then incorporated into specific TDI combinations to derive the corresponding response function. This paper introduces a generalized formulation for TDI combinations based on multiple geometric links. By extending the representation of the laser Doppler frequency shift to include various geometric configurations, such as round-trip and non-round-trip links, we reformulate 45 second-generation TDI combinations. For several of these, the new formulation significantly streamlines their mathematical expressions and enhances physical clarity. Our results demonstrate that the proposed link-mapping rules not only enable efficient construction of response functions for these TDI combinations but also reduce computational complexity. This approach provides a reliable theoretical and algorithmic foundation for data processing in future space-borne GW missions.

### [31] [Nonlinear stability of subextremal Kerr black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28253)
*Peter Hintz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在完全次极端范围内，Kerr黑洞族在爱因斯坦真空方程下的全局非线性稳定性：初始数据接近次极端Kerr黑洞的时空，在空间紧致区域内以速率 $\mathcal{O}(t_*^{-2-\varepsilon_{\mathcal K}})$ 衰减到邻近的Kerr成员。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Kerr黑洞在完全次极端范围内的全局非线性稳定性问题，这是广义相对论中一个长期未解决的核心问题。

Method: 采用推广的波映射规范，通过规范源项进行修正；将规范源项与最终黑洞参数、引力波尾迹一起作为未知量，纳入非线性Nash-Moser迭代方案；直接处理张量方程，不依赖简化为标量方程（线性模稳定性证明除外）；依赖两篇姊妹论文分别提供约束阻尼和波动方程的tame估计。

Result: 证明了从接近次极端Kerr黑洞的初始数据出发的时空，最终会衰减到邻近的Kerr黑洞成员，衰减率为 $\mathcal{O}(t_*^{-2-\varepsilon_{\mathcal K}})$（空间紧致区域）。

Conclusion: 建立了Kerr黑洞在完全次极端范围内的全局非线性稳定性，这是该领域的一个重要里程碑。

Abstract: We settle the global nonlinear stability problem for the family of Kerr black holes in the full subextremal range: spacetimes evolving from initial data close to those of a subextremal Kerr black hole as solutions of the Einstein vacuum equation ${\rm Ric}(g)=0$ settle down to a nearby member of the Kerr family at the rate $\mathcal{O}(t_*^{-2-ε_{\mathcal K}})$ in spatially compact regions.
  For the initial data, we require $\mathcal{O}(r^{-1-ε_0})$-decay for $ε_0>0$ -- more precisely, an arbitrary but finite expansion into terms $r^{-z}(\log r)^k$ where $z>1$, $k\in\mathbb{N}_0$, plus a remainder term with $\mathcal{O}(r^{-3-ε_0})$-decay. Similarly to previous work with Vasy in the Kerr-de Sitter setting, we use a generalized wave map gauge modified using gauge source terms that lie in a suitable finite-dimensional space determined by the expansion of the initial data. Like the final black hole parameters (mass and angular momentum) and the gravitational wave tail, the gauge source terms are treated as unknowns in a nonlinear (Nash-Moser) iteration scheme. We work directly with the tensorial equation and in particular do not rely on reductions to scalar equations (except insofar as a reduction to the Teukolsky equation is used in the proof of linear mode stability).
  This paper relies on two companion papers by the author. The first one introduces a strong form of constraint damping in the full subextremal range, which we use in our formulation of the gauge-fixed Einstein equation as a black box. The second one provides tame estimates (albeit with weak decay) for forward solutions of a general class of wave-type equations, which we show here to include the linearizations of the gauge-fixed Einstein equation arising in our nonlinear iteration scheme; these estimates are the starting point for our detailed asymptotic analysis.

</details>


### [32] [Generalizing the interacting dilatonic ghost condensate as a dark energy model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28288)
*Manuel Gonzalez-Espinoza,Ramon Herrera,Johan Casimiro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个广义膨胀鬼凝聚场作为暗能量候选者的宇宙演化，该场由包含两个主导动能项（一个线性项和一个任意整数n>2项）与指数势的拉格朗日密度构建，并与暗物质通过源项相互作用。分析了非相互作用Q=0及两种相互作用模型（Q∝ρ_m\dotφ和Q∝ρ_m H），通过相空间分析获得稳定性条件，并利用宇宙计时器、PantheonPlus和DESI观测数据进行联合似然分析，给出了n=3和n=5时的参数约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索广义膨胀鬼凝聚场作为暗能量候选者的宇宙演化，并研究其与暗物质的不同相互作用形式对宇宙动力学的影响。

Method: 采用拉格朗日密度构建广义膨胀鬼凝聚场模型，包含线性动能项和n>2的高阶动能项以及指数势；分别考虑Q=0、Q∝ρ_m\dotφ和Q∝ρ_m H三种相互作用情形；进行相空间动力学分析确定临界点和稳定性条件；利用宇宙计时器、PantheonPlus和DESI观测数据进行联合似然分析，在68%和95%置信水平下对n=3和n=5情形进行参数约束。

Result: 所有情形下系统都能复现标准宇宙学动力学，并演化至以暗能量为主的晚期吸引子，展现出类Quintessence或Phantom特征（取决于标准动能项耦合参数α的符号）。对于Q∝\dotφρ_m相互作用，能量流动方向取决于α的符号；而对于Q∝Hρ_m相互作用，能量流动方向与α符号无关，始终为从暗物质向暗能量转移。

Conclusion: 广义膨胀鬼凝聚场模型能有效描述暗能量演化，不同相互作用形式会导致不同的能量转移行为，观测数据可对模型参数施加约束。

Abstract: In this article, we study the cosmic evolution of a generalized dilatonic ghost condensate field as a dark energy candidate, formulated from a Lagrangian density with two dominant kinetic terms; one linear and one of arbitrary integer $n>2$ in combination with an exponential potential, which interacts with dark matter through a source term. We analyzed three scenarios: the non-interacting situation $Q=0$ and two different interaction models, $Q\proptoρ_m\dotφ$ and $Q\propto ρ_m H$ to describe the evolution of the present universe. For each interaction $Q$, we perform a detailed phase-space analysis to obtain stability conditions and identify critical points. In all situations, the system reproduces the standard cosmological dynamics and evolves toward late-time dark energy-dominated attractors, with quintessence or phantom features depending on the sign of the coupling parameter $α$ associated with the standard kinetic term. Furthermore, a joint likelihood analysis with Cosmic Chronometers, PantheonPlus, and DESI observations is performed for two values of power $n$ ($n=3$ and $n=5$) to determine marginalized parameter constraints at the confidence levels of 68$\%$ and 95$\%$ for the different $Q-$models. For the interaction term $Q\propto \dotφρ_m$, we find that the direction of the flow of energy depends on the sign of the coupling parameter $α$ associated with the standard kinetic term. However, for the interaction $Q\propto H\,ρ_m$, the direction of the energy flow is independent of the sign of the coupling parameter $α$ and always remains negative, corresponding to an energy transfer from dark matter to dark energy.

</details>

### [33] [Zonal Spherical Functions of Quantum Symmetric Pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27901)
*Philip Schlösser*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文为量子对称对中的区域球函数和特征球函数建立了与Koornwinder-Macdonald对称多项式的联系，将Letzter (2004)的方法推广到现代框架、右余理想子代数、非标准情形及非既约限制根系，并对FII型提出了猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Letzter (2004)的方法现代化并扩展到更一般的情形（非标准情形、非既约限制根系），以统一刻画量子对称对中的球函数与Koornwinder-Macdonald多项式之间的联系。

Method: 采用Letzter (2004)的方法论，将其翻译到现代约定和右余理想子代数框架下，并推广到非标准情形以及非既约限制根系的情形。

Result: 成功识别了量子对称对中的区域球函数和特征球函数与对称Koornwinder-Macdonald多项式的对应关系，并对最后一个未解决的Satake类型FII提出了猜想。

Conclusion: 完成了量子对称对球函数与Koornwinder-Macdonald多项式之间联系的系统性建立，填补了FII型这一空白。

Abstract: We identify the zonal and character spherical functions for quantum symmetric pairs with the symmetric Koornwinder--Macdonald polynomials. To this end, the methods of Letzter's 2004 paper are translated to modern conventions and right coideal subalgebras, and extended to non-standard cases and cases with non-reduced restricted root systems. For the last elusive Satake type, FII, a conjecture is provided.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化黎曼平面上测地线发散程度，并建立一种在拟等距下保持不变的紧化方式，同时将拟重定向边界与Martin边界联系起来。

Method: 利用Qing-Rafi提出的拟重定向概念推广Gromov边界化；研究渐进锥的性质；分析Laplace-Beltrami算子对应的Martin边界。

Abstract: In this article, we study Riemannian planes $(M,g)$ which satisfies a certain bounded geometry condition and geodesic divergence on these Riemannian planes. We recall quasi-redirection (introduced by Qing and Rafi) which generalises Gromov's bordification for $δ-$hyperbolic spaces and use it to quantify geodesic divergence in a manner which is invariant under quasi-isometries. We use it to compactify Riemannian planes into either $\mathbb{D}^2$ or $\mathbb{S}^2$ depending on how fast geodesics on $(M,g)$ spread apart. We study asymptotic cones of Riemannian planes and use them to come up with necessary and sufficient conditions for the quasi-redirecting compactification being $\mathbb{S}^2$ in terms of it admitting a proper asymptotic cone . Lastly, we study the Martin boundary of Riemannian planes ( with respect to the Laplace-Beltrami operator $Δ_g$) in relation to the quasi-redirecting boundary and show that if the quasi-redirecting boundary is homeomorphic to the Martin boundary, then the identity map on $(M,g)$ induces a homeomorphism from the quasi-redirecting compactification of $(M,g)$ to the Martin compactification of $(M,g)$.

### [40] [Bottleneck Effects and Harmonic-Type Velocity Bounds for Periodic Quantum Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27740)
*Houssam Abdul-Rahman,Thomas A. Jackson,Darren C. Ong*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We prove explicit upper bounds on the propagation velocity of one-dimensional quantum walks with periodic coins of arbitrary period. We treat two complementary settings. First, in a perturbative regime where one transmission parameter is small, we show that the corresponding almost reflecting coin acts as a bottleneck for transport: the velocity is bounded linearly in this parameter, with an explicit leading order estimate. Second, for arbitrary nonzero transmission parameters, we prove a general a priori bound in terms of their harmonic mean, together with a refined version that detects the spatial variation of neighboring coins. Moreover, we prove a general lower bound on the velocity. These bounds apply directly to the corresponding CMV setting.

### [41] [Uniqueness, analyticity and mixing for Gibbs point processes via spectral gaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28009)
*Andreas Göbel,Matthew Jenssen,Marcus Michelen,Marcus Pappik,Will Perkins,Leon Schiller*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究吉布斯点过程在连续体中的相互作用，定义了谱阈值λ_spec，证明了在阈值以下活动性范围内无限体积吉布斯测度的唯一性、压力的解析性以及时空混合性质。对于硬球模型，改进了现有唯一性和解析性界限，在高维情况下指数级提升。还证明了硬球模型热浴动力学的最优混合时间。此外，展示了某些排斥势的λ_spec=+∞，表明无相变，特别在8维和24维中，无相变势的基态由E_8和Leech晶格给出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 改进硬球模型及其他排斥势模型在吉布斯点过程中的相变界限，确立谱阈值λ_spec作为统一框架，并探索高维情况下的渐近行为以及特殊维度中的无相变势。

Method: 基于Kondratiev-Kuna-Ohlerich 2013年关于谱间隙的工作，将谱阈值λ_spec作为核心概念，通过证明谱间隙蕴含无相变的各种强形式，并针对硬球势和特殊排斥势分析λ_spec的行为。

Result: 1) 在λ_spec以下证明了唯一性、解析性和混合性；2) 改进硬球模型的界限，高维时指数级提升；3) 硬球模型热浴动力学混合时间最优界限（期望密度Θ(d/2^d)）；4) 展示某些排斥势λ_spec=+∞，无相变；5) 在8维和24维中，无相变势的基态由E_8和Leech晶格给出。

Conclusion: 谱阈值λ_spec为研究吉布斯点过程相变提供了统一框架，有效改进了硬球模型界限，并揭示了特殊维度中晶格与无相变势的深刻联系。

Abstract: A Gibbs point process models particles interacting in the continuum through a potential. Among the most classical examples is the hard-sphere model, where given an activity parameter $λ$, a radius $r$, and a bounded set $Λ\subset \mathbb{R}^d$ one samples a Poisson process of intensity $λ$ in $Λ$ conditioned on the points forming the centers of an $r$-sphere packing. We prove uniqueness of infinite-volume Gibbs measure, analyticity of the pressure, and various notions of spatial and temporal mixing for activities up to what we define as the spectral threshold $λ_{spec}$ of the potential. For each fixed dimension $d \geq 2$, this improves the uniqueness and analyticity bounds for the hard-sphere model. As $d \to \infty$, our improvement over the classical bounds grows exponentially. We also prove an optimal mixing time bound for heat bath dynamics for the hard-sphere model up to an expected density of $Θ(d / 2^d)$, the first result that asymptotically matches the maximum density for rapid mixing predicted by Parisi and Zamponi.
  We also exhibit repulsive, radial pair potentials for which $λ_{spec} = + \infty$, showing that the corresponding Gibbs point processes have no phase transition at any activity $λ> 0$. Further, in dimensions $8$ and $24$ we exhibit such a potential with no phase transition for which the work of Cohn-Kumar-Miller-Radchenko-Viazovska proves that the unique ground state at any fixed density is given by the $E_8$ and Leech lattices, respectively. Our work builds upon a 2013 work of Kondratiev-Kuna-Ohlerich that implicitly defined $λ_{spec}$ and proved a spectral gap for a Glauber-like continuum birth-death dynamics. Our main work shows that such a spectral gap implies several strong notions of absence of phase transition and analyzes the behavior of $λ_{spec}$ for interesting potentials.

</details>

### [43] [Which Saddles Contribute? The South-East Rule for Multidimensional Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28271)
*Inês Aniceto,Job Feldbrugge,Christopher J. Howls*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于几何的简单算法，用于确定多重积分渐近展开中贡献的关键临界点（包括实和复），通过结合三个特征：Borel平面上临界点的函数值、基于代数复兴的邻接概念，以及新提出的"东南"几何规则，避免了传统Picard-Lefschetz方法中计算复流线的需求。该算法对处理Wick旋转问题和路径积分中的瞬子贡献识别具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Picard-Lefschetz方法需要计算$\mathbb C^d$中$-\text{Re} (i\nabla f)$的流线来识别相关临界点，计算复杂度高。作者希望开发一种更简单、系统的几何算法来替代这一过程，为实时间路径积分中瞬子贡献的系统识别提供基础。

Method: 算法结合三个核心要素：(1) 在复Borel平面上绘制所有临界点处的$f$值；(2) 利用代数复兴/超渐近方法导出临界点之间的邻接关系；(3) 新提出的几何"东南"规则，用于判断哪些临界点实际贡献于渐近展开。该算法适用于$\mathbb R^d$上有界或无界的函数$f$。

Result: 通过教学性和高级示例展示了该算法的有效性，证明了其能够正确识别贡献的临界点，且无需计算复杂的复流线。算法成功处理了有界和无界函数的情形。

Conclusion: 该算法是向系统地识别实时间路径积分中瞬子贡献的重要一步，对解决Wick旋转相关问题具有重要意义。它提供了一种比Picard-Lefschetz方法更简洁的替代方案，有望在路径积分等物理应用中得到广泛使用。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce and demonstrate a simple geometric algorithm to determine which critical points, both complex as well as real, contribute to the asymptotic evaluation of multiple integrals with exponential integrands of the form $e^{ikf(\boldsymbol{x})}$ over $\mathbb R^d$, for finite $d\ge 1$ and $f$ is analytic. In so doing, the algorithm removes the need to compute the flows of $-\text{Re} (i\nabla f)$ in $\mathbb C^d$ that is required to identify such relevant critical points in Picard-Lefschetz approaches to the derivation of such asymptotic expansions. By contrast, our algorithm relies on the combination of three simple features: the values of $f$ at all the critical points plotted in the complex Borel plane, the concept of adjacency between such points derived from algebraic resurgence/hyperasymptotic approaches and the new result here of a geometric "South-East" rule. The algorithm incorporates functions $f$ that remain bounded or unbounded on $\mathbb R^d$. We illustrate this new approach with both pedagogical and advanced examples, and draw conclusions as to its importance for resolving issues associated with Wick rotations and its implications for path integrals. This is a significant step towards a systematic way of identifying instanton contributions in real-time path integrals.

</details>

### [44] [Range-controlled entanglement in Lindbladian skin states of monitored fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09306)

TL;DR: 本文研究受监测的费米子链中，通过粒子数守恒的定向耗散实现林德布拉德皮肤态，发现短程跳迁导致完全皮肤积累和面积律纠缠，而长程跳迁产生有限体态尾部与次体积律纠缠，揭示了耗散与相干跳迁对皮肤局域化和量子纠缠的协同控制。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平衡态中，相空间概率分布（如Wigner函数）是解析的；本文旨在探索这一性质在驱动耗散系统中是否依然成立，并揭示非平衡稳态中罕有涨落的统计行为。

Method: 以参数驱动的Kerr振子为模型，考虑线性和/或非线性耦合到耗散浴；采用Keldysh-Lindblad作用量的半经典瞬时子轨迹方法，分析幅度和相位中的罕有涨落。

Result: 发现驱动耗散系统的大偏差函数普遍存在非解析性（导数不连续的线/面）；同一涨落可由多个不同的瞬时子轨迹实现；这些轨迹之间的竞争导致主导瞬时子的突然切换，从而产生大偏差函数的非解析特征。

Conclusion: 驱动开放量子系统稳态中罕有涨落的统计性质与平衡态有本质区别，大偏差函数的非解析性是其普适特征，源自多瞬时子轨迹的竞争与切换。

Abstract: We study statistics of atypical measurement outcomes in the steady states of driven open quantum systems. In equilibrium, the probability distribution over the phase space, as encoded in, e.g., the Wigner function, is analytic in the phase-space coordinates. We show that this property is generically lost in driven dissipative systems: their {\it large-deviation function} develops lines and surfaces across which its derivatives are discontinuous. As an illustrative example, we consider a parametrically driven Kerr oscillator coupled linearly and/or nonlinearly to a dissipative bath. Rare fluctuations in the amplitude and phase of the induced oscillations are governed by semiclassical instanton trajectories of the corresponding Keldysh-Lindblad action. We demonstrate that a given fluctuation can be realized through multiple distinct instanton trajectories. The competition between these trajectories leads to abrupt switching of the dominant instanton and, consequently, to non-analytic features in the large-deviation function.

### [48] [Reservoir-independent lossless charging and protected storage of an open quantum battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27403)

Abstract: A quantum battery charged through a lossy intermediate state faces a structural trade-off between charging speed and dissipation. We show that an exact algebraic cancellation removes it in a driven three-level cell: the radiatively decaying state is fed by a single bright amplitude, and a counterdiabatic field annuls the lone residual source that drives it, holding the lossy state identically empty. Charging is then lossless -- not one photon is emitted through the bridge -- at any one-photon detuning, coupling, linewidth, and speed down to the rotating-wave limit, with no adiabatic elimination, so the charging power is bounded by the drive amplitude (a quantum speed limit) rather than by dissipation. Crucially, this losslessness is independent of the reservoir: because the dark sector never engages the system-bath coupling, the emission vanishes exactly for an arbitrary spectral density, Markovian or not, as an exact damped-pseudomode treatment confirms to machine precision across all memory times. The entire non-Hermitian structure -- a Markovian second-order exceptional point that reservoir memory promotes to a third-order one, and the attendant dissipation phase diagram -- lives in the bright sector, from which the protocol is by construction exempt. This inverts dissipation-engineered charging, where an exceptional point or reservoir memory is a resource; here the lossy sector is never populated at all. The same dark-state structure protects the stored charge, converting fast radiative self-discharge into the slow metastable lifetime, with residuals quadratic in the control error. We detail experimental requirements and representative parameters for neutral alkaline-earth atoms, trapped ions, transmons, and defect centers.

### [49] [Compression-Driven Anomaly Detection in Brain MRI Using an Interpretable Quantum Autoencoder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27411)

Method: 采用角度编码将图像块映射到量子态空间，构建变分量子编码器-解码器架构，通过辅助垃圾量子比特实现信息丢弃训练。异常分数基于输入数据相对于正常数据分布的压缩难度计算，分数越高表示异常程度越大。

Abstract: We study a quantum autoencoder (QAE) for compression-driven anomaly detection in brain MRI data. Anomaly scores reflect the degree to which inputs resist compression relative to normal data, with higher scores corresponding to deviations from the learned normal manifold. Analysis of the learned parameters reveals a pronounced encoder-decoder asymmetry, where effective anomaly detection arises from structured information compression within the encoder rather than increased parameter magnitude or decoder expressivity. This results in a controlled compression-reconstruction trade-off with a clear operating regime that supports principled threshold selection. Qualitative evaluation further shows that the QAE produces spatially localized anomaly heatmaps aligned with tumorous regions. The results, supported by promising baseline performances, demonstrate that quantum autoencoders provide an interpretable and controllable mechanism for anomaly detection based on incompressibility with respect to a learned latent representation. This work highlights the potential of quantum autoencoders as a principled tool for studying compression dynamics in quantum machine learning, with promising implications for decision support in medical imaging workflows.

### [50] [Fault tolerant computation of the static structure factor and finite size effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27734)
*Rishabh Bhardwaj,Alexander Reed Muñoz,Travis E. Jones,John Golden*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种量子后处理策略，用于纠正在周期材料基态能量估计中由有限尺寸效应引起的两体误差。该方法通过Bloch轨道基下的结构因子测量来实现，成本低于主量子算法，为有限尺寸校正提供了容错替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 通过扭转平均减少单体壳效应后，残留误差由长波密度涨落控制，编码在小动量静态结构因子S(q)中；(2) 在Bloch轨道基下构建结构因子算符，通过密度算符实现块编码；(3) 使用放大的Hadamard测试估算基态期望值；(4) 引入自适应全局和局部二分搜索，确定用于重建两体有限尺寸误差校正的红外拟合窗口。

Result: 结构因子校正的主成本为ÑO(N_b N_k)^3，依赖于Bloch轨道基大小，避免了全哈密顿量模拟的大平面波预因子，仅需ÑO(N_b N_k)逻辑量子比特。该成本相对于主基态能量估计程序是次主导的。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了下采样（down-sampling）的容错替代方案，将重复在更大晶胞上计算能量替换为对控制有限尺寸效应的红外密度相关性的定向测量。

Abstract: Fault-tolerant quantum algorithms offer a promising pathway for estimating the ground-state energies of periodic materials that are beyond the practical reach of classical electronic-structure methods. A remaining challenge is finite-size mitigation: quantum algorithms evaluate a finite supercell or finite Brillouin-zone mesh, while materials properties are defined in the thermodynamic limit. In this work we develop a quantum post-processing strategy for the leading two-body finite-size correction. After one-body shell effects are reduced by twist averaging, the dominant residual error is controlled by long-wavelength density fluctuations, which are encoded in the small-momentum static structure factor $S(q)$. We formulate the corresponding operator in a Bloch-orbital basis, construct its block encoding through the density operator, and estimate its ground-state expectation value using an amplified Hadamard test. We also introduce adaptive global and local binary search procedures for identifying the infrared fitting window used to reconstruct the two-body finite size error correction. The resulting cost remains subleading relative to the main ground-state energy estimation routine: the structure-factor correction has leading $\tilde{O}(N_bN_k)^3$ dependence on the Bloch-orbital basis size, avoids the large plane-wave prefactor of full Hamiltonian simulation, and requires only $\tilde{O}(N_bN_k)$ logical qubits. This provides a fault-tolerant alternative to down-sampling, replacing repeated energy calculations on larger cells with targeted measurements of the infrared density correlations that control the finite-size effects.

Abstract: Non-Hermitian Hamiltonians are a fascinating class of many-body models that describe the effective dynamics of quantum systems interacting with the environment through particle, energy, or information exchange. Although their theoretical framework is well established, the controlled engineering of such Hamiltonians in the context of quantum simulations remains challenging, even more so when the non-Hermitian part describes a $k$-body interaction. Qudit quantum simulators offer a compelling framework to implement such models. We theoretically investigate the dynamics of a one-dimensional chain of qudits undergoing hybrid unitary-projective evolution, where suitably designed measurements constrain the dynamics to a Zeno subspace. As we illustrate for the case of qutrits, within the Zeno subspace the dynamics is governed by an effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian for an ensemble of pseudo-spins $1/2$, which can inherit non-Hermitian two-body interactions with the same connectivity as the full qutrit chain. We derive an analytical relation linking the monitored qutrits' evolution to a desired target non-Hermitian Hamiltonian and validate the effective description through numerical simulations of a representative model. Our scheme provides a constructive route for the realization of a large class of interacting non-Hermitian many-body Hamiltonians in experimentally relevant multilevel quantum platforms, including trapped ions and superconducting circuits.

Here we report thousands of monolithic semiconductor quantum-dot devices fabricated using a III--V pilot production-line process compatible with large-scale deployment. Systematic control of source parameters yields state-of-the-art efficiency and supports a path to optical losses below fault-tolerance thresholds. Abstract: The classification of mixed-state phases requires criteria beyond two-point correlation functions, such as the decay of the mutual information (MI) and the conditional mutual information (CMI), with the latter encapsulated in the notion of Markov length. Here we show how such static properties of the fixed point of a Lindbladian follow from natural dynamical features of its generators: rapid mixing and frustration-freeness. We focus on systems with long-range interactions, and prove (i) that local Lindbladians satisfying (global) rapid mixing and frustration-freeness have fixed-points whose CMI decays with the shielding distance, and (ii) that (local) rapid mixing together with primitivity and regularity implies global decay of MI. For long-range interactions decaying with a power law with rate $α$, both quantities decay polynomially rather than exponentially, in contrast to the finite- and short-range regimes where exponential decay (a finite Markov length) is expected within a phase. We further show that Gibbs states of long-range, non-commuting Hamiltonians satisfy a local Markov property at any temperatures, extending the recent results (Chen--Rouzé, 2025) for short-range systems to the long-range regime relevant to a variety of experimental platforms. As a numerical example, we study the long-range Ising model both with and without a transverse field. We find regimes in which the polynomial decay of the CMI holds, in accordance with the bounds proven.

Abstract: We present a method for simulating operator dynamics in out-of-equilibrium quantum systems. Due to the rapid growth of complexity in these systems, this is typically speaking an intractable task. However, exceptional progress has been made in recent years to sidestep this barrier, with the introduction of a number of methods that make use of a truncation of the simulation to low-weight (the number of non-trivial terms in a Pauli string basis expansion) observables, which turns out to be a good approximation for many dynamical quantities of interest, e.g., two-point infinite-temperature correlation functions between local operators. In this work, we extend this idea to a leaner truncation protocol, truncating operators based on their diameter - that is, the size of the region on the lattice on which they are non-trivially supported. Result: TR方法在标准绝热动力学失效的演化时间内仍能保持高基态保真度，且对系统尺寸依赖较弱；实现了多体系统中GHZ态的高保真制备，扩展了固定演化时间内可达到的系统尺寸；证明了Mandelstam-Tamm量子速度极限不构成TR加速的根本限制。

Conclusion: TR方法是一种可扩展且实验可行的多体系统快速量子控制方案。

Abstract: Fast quantum control is essential to overcome decoherence in contemporary quantum platforms, yet achieving this in many-body systems remains a major challenge. We show that the time-rescaling (TR) method enables efficient acceleration of closed many-body quantum dynamics, extending its applicability beyond previously studied regimes. Applying TR to the transverse-field Ising model with a longitudinal field, we demonstrate a significant enhancement of quantum annealing performance, maintaining high ground-state fidelity at evolution times where standard adiabatic dynamics breaks down, with only weak dependence on system size. We further demonstrate high-fidelity preparation of Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger states in many-body systems, where TR extends the accessible system sizes within fixed evolution times. We additionally show that the Mandelstam-Tamm quantum speed limit does not fundamentally limit the acceleration achievable through TR, as the reduction in evolution time is exactly compensated by increased energy fluctuations. These results establish TR as a scalable and experimentally viable approach to fast quantum control in many-body systems.

Abstract: Squared commutators in the Holstein--Primakoff limit of a spin--cavity system provide a compact way to separate propagation from covariance growth in a finite-temperature reservoir with memory. In the finite-temperature NMQSD construction, the linear quadrature commutator is fixed by the retarded spin--cavity propagator, whereas a quadratic commutator carries the same retarded factor together with a covariance factor. For a zero-mean Gaussian state, \(C_{R_i^2,R_j}(t)=4|κ_{ij}(t)|^2V_{ii}(t)\); the symmetrized expression gives the spin-side and mixed channels. Since \(\bar n\) enters the covariance sector but not the homogeneous retarded kernel, raising \(\bar n\) from 0 to 1 leaves the linear transfer unchanged while increasing the quadratic signal. Varying the bath-memory rate and the counter-rotating coupling within the stable HP region then shows how stored cavity history changes both the transfer weight and its distribution in time. The calculation separates memory-dependent propagation from thermal covariance growth in collective spin--cavity dynamics.

Two prominent examples of SMC tasks are sealed-bid auction and secure multi-party summation.
