In this work, structural symmetries in existing protocols for quantum auction and quantum summation are identified. In particular, it is established that the core auction primitives including revenue estimation, maximum bid identification, and winner determination can be reduced to repeated invocations of a summation oracle acting on suitably defined indicator functions. Conversely, summation protocols can be naturally embedded as auxiliary subroutines within auction frameworks, establishing summation as a unifying primitive underlying a broad class of auction mechanisms. Further, computational, communication and memory costs of these reductions are analyzed and compared with some of the representative existing protocols. The proposed framework is protocol-agnostic and applicable across diverse computational models, including gate-based and photonic implementations. Here, the fundamental laws governing the cloning of quantum ensembles are investigated. This stands in sharp contrast to the conventional no-cloning theorem, which relies on the state being unknown. By revisiting the fundamental principles of optical interference, this work reveals that interference in TF QKD inherently relies only on the instantaneous phase alignment of two independent optical pulses at the moment they temporally overlap, rather than on continuous global phase synchronization. Guided by this insight, we propose and demonstrate a single-sideband-interference TF-QKD protocol that eliminates global phase locking. Each user employs an IQ modulator to generate a weak single sideband as the quantum signal, while the intrinsically phase-correlated optical carrier propagates as a real-time phase reference. Carrier interference at the receiver enables real-time phase extraction and feedback compensation for the sidebands. Unlike prior no phase locking approaches requiring second- or microsecond-level coherence, in principle, our scheme reduces this requirement to nanoseconds. Here we propose and analyze a time-reversed Young--Afshar configuration in which the corresponding null test is transferred from the downstream field plane to the source-label plane of a time-reversed Young interferometer. In this reciprocal geometry, a point-addressable source illuminates a double slit, while the detector remains fixed. The observed fringe is therefore not a single-shot spatial intensity pattern, but a detector-conditioned response reconstructed by scanning the source coordinate. Consequently, a null in this pattern is not a node of a freely propagating field; it is a source label for which the coherent two-slit transfer amplitude to the selected detector vanishes. A mask placed at such source-plane labels is invisible to that detector when both slits are open, yet becomes visible when either slit is opened alone. We develop the scalar Fresnel model, derive the source-space null condition, introduce a detector-conditioned null-mask loss, and examine how this loss evolves under a tunable which-path marker. The source-space visibility and path distinguishability satisfy the standard duality relation, so no violation of complementarity is implied. The essential new feature is instead a reciprocal, detector-conditioned form of complementarity: Afshar's field-space transparency is replaced by response-function transparency in a reconstructed source basis.

Motivation: 流量矩阵（TM）预测是流量工程的核心，但在内存、更新和训练预算受限的在线网络控制场景下，实现准确的全矩阵预测仍具挑战。现有依赖图、Transformer或扩散模块的方法开销过高。

Method: 将门控量子启发式Kolmogorov-Arnold网络快速权重编程器（QKAN-FWP）适配到Abilene TM多步预测任务。每个模型从2小时历史预测后续20个5分钟帧（共144通道OD矩阵）。对比三种QKAN放置变体、匹配规模LSTM、更大LSTM及经典门控快速权重编程器，在固定预算训练协议下评估。

Result: G-QKANFWP在循环模型中取得最佳RMSE，参数量仅为大LSTM的22.4%；优于匹配规模LSTM和经典G-FWP基线；量子启发变体在验证损失AULC和OD通道胜率上均优于匹配规模基线。G-QKANFWP和GQKAN-FWP在OD通道胜率上表现突出。

Conclusion: 经典慢编程器结合量子启发式快速编程器是一种有前景的精度-效率协同设计，适用于资源受限的网络流量矩阵预测任务。

Abstract: Traffic matrices (TMs) capture network-wide origin-destination demand and are central to traffic engineering, yet accurate whole-matrix forecasting remains challenging when prediction must be performed under the memory, update, and training-budget constraints of online network control. This paper investigates whether compact quantum-inspired recurrent models can provide effective TM forecasts without relying on dedicated graph, transformer, or diffusion modules. We adapt gated quantum-inspired Kolmogorov-Arnold network fast-weight programmers (QKAN-FWPs) to direct multi-step Abilene TM forecasting, where each model predicts the next 20 five-minute frames of a 144-channel origin-destination (OD) matrix from a two-hour history. We benchmark three QKAN placement variants against a matched-size long short-term memory (LSTM) network, a larger LSTM, and a classical gated fast-weight programmer under a shared fixed-budget training protocol. Among the evaluated recurrent models, G-QKANFWP achieves the best pooled root-mean-square error (RMSE), while using only 22.4% of the larger LSTM. It also outperforms both the matched-size LSTM and the classical G-FWP baseline, indicating that the gain is not due to gated fast-weight framework alone. Convergence and channel-wise analyses further show that the quantum-inspired variants obtain lower validation-loss area under the learning curve (AULC) than matched-size recurrent baselines, while G-QKANFWP and GQKAN-FWP achieve substantially more OD-channel wins. These results identify a classical slow programmer with a quantum-inspired fast programmer as a promising accuracy-efficiency design for resource-conscious network traffic-matrix forecasting.

Method: 采用量子幅度调制连续波架构，信号光子直接照射目标，闲频光子经高频余弦波非局域调制且不接触目标，利用非局域调制与量子关联实现目标探测。

Abstract: Quantum light detection and ranging (LiDAR) utilizes quantum entanglement and correlation to improve precision, noise resilience and covertness of target detection. Despite recent advances, the development of a quantum LiDAR system that simultaneously achieves high precision and a large measurement range remains challenging. Here, we demonstrate a quantum amplitude-modulated continuous wave LiDAR with micrometer precision achievable via increased acquisition time and meter-scale measurement range. In our demonstration, the signal photons directly illuminate the target, while the idler photons are non-locally modulated with a high-frequency cosine wave and never interact with the target. By leveraging the non-local modulation and the quantum correlation, the target detection is achieved with a precision of 0.64 $\pm$ 0.06 mm within one second over a measurement range of 2-8 m. As the acquisition time is up to 500 s, the system achieves a precision of 29 $\pm\ 4{\ \mathrm{μm}}$. Furthermore, our system realizes a 50 times precision improvement over the classical single-photon scheme in a background noise 37 dB stronger than the returned probe photons. With these advantages, our method will open venues for the development of high-precision, long-range, and noise-resilient target detection.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子碰撞模型在量子计算机上实现马尔可夫量子动力学面临噪声、电路深度、辅助比特重置开销和量子比特资源限制等挑战，此前实验仅限于1-2个系统量子比特和少于12个时间步长，亟需更大规模、更多步长的实验验证。

Method: 采用量子碰撞模型，将系统耦合到辅助比特以实现耗散；针对离子阱和超导量子计算机分别设计硬件特定的辅助比特策略，实现局域和非局域耗散下的马尔可夫量子过程模拟。

Abstract: Hamiltonian dynamics have been widely implemented on noisy intermediate-scale quantum devices in recent years. In contrast, experimental demonstrations of Markovian quantum dynamics remain limited, because implementing nonunitary evolution on quantum computers is challenging. Quantum collision models provide a natural approach to this problem by coupling the system to ancillas to realize dissipation. However, previous implementations of quantum collision models on quantum computers have typically been restricted to one or two system qubits and fewer than 12 time steps, owing to noise, circuit depth, the overhead of ancilla reset, and limited qubit resources. In this work, we experimentally simulate Markovian quantum processes with local and nonlocal dissipation on both trapped-ion and superconducting quantum computers. By employing hardware-specific ancilla strategies, we realize simulations with up to seven system qubits, corresponding to 13 qubits in total, and 40 time steps. Our results demonstrate that, even for the same physical model, the optimal implementation strategy depends strongly on the hardware characteristics of the quantum computer.

Abstract: Vector polarimetry is an important application frontier for Rydberg-atom-based sensing. Here we propose a theoretical framework for high-sensitivity detection of radio-frequency (RF) electric field polarization direction, which is particularly suitable for weak-field detection. Under a static magnetic field, the asymmetry in coupling between the Zeeman sublevels of the Rydberg atom and the RF field's polarization components enables the polarization angles to be determined from the atomic absorption index, which is retrieved via homodyne detection by incorporating the Rydberg atom system into an SU(1,1) interferometer. We derive the sensitivity of the polarization angles along with the corresponding standard quantum limit (SQL) and quantum Cramér--Rao bound (QCRB). Our results demonstrate a sensitivity surpassing the SQL across wide angular ranges using either dual coherent states or a coherent state combined with a squeezed vacuum state as input. Significantly, the optimal sensitivity reaches below \SI{e-6}{\degree}, with sensitivities better than \SI{e-3}{\degree} maintained over most of the angular domain. This work establishes a foundation for high-precision vector polarimetry, thereby advancing the development of Rydberg-atom-based quantum sensing and contributing to a deeper understanding of light--matter interactions.

### [74] [Non-equilibrium quantum thermometry with bosonic samples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27894)
*Marek Winczewski,Michał Horodecki,Ricard Ravell Rodríguez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究使用玻色探针（量子谐振子）在低温非平衡态下进行量子测温，对比了强耦合非马尔可夫动力学与马尔可夫主方程方法。发现非马尔可夫情况下量子Fisher信息（QFI）随时间非单调，存在最优有限测量时间；而马尔可夫情况下QFI单调趋于稳态，最优时间在无穷远。压缩初态可提供瞬态优势，强耦合可缓解低温指数抑制问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究低温非平衡态下强耦合、非马尔可夫效应对量子测温精度的影响，尤其是探索有限时间最优测量策略及克服低温Boltzmann指数抑制的途径。

Method: 采用Boyanovsky和Jasnow的二次型精确解处理探针-浴动力学，以及重整化GKLS主方程。从时间依赖的协方差矩阵提取单模高斯探针态（包括压缩态）的量子Fisher信息。

Result: 强耦合非马尔可夫情形下QFI呈非单调时间演化，存在有限最优测量时间；马尔可夫情形下QFI单调递增至稳态，最优时间趋于无穷。压缩初态提供瞬态优势但被热化抹平。平衡态下强耦合将低温度相对误差的指数Boltzmann抑制替换为更温和的多项式发散。

Conclusion: 压缩和测量时间是互补的测温资源；强耦合非马尔可夫效应可改善低温测温精度；该模型可直接映射到电路QED实验，方案具备实验可行性。

Abstract: We study low-temperature non-equilibrium quantum thermometry with a bosonic probe: a quantum harmonic oscillator strongly coupled to a bosonic bath at temperature $T$ through a Drude--Ohmic spectral density. We treat the probe--bath dynamics both exactly, using the quadratic solution of Boyanovsky and Jasnow, and within a renormalized Gorini--Kossakowski--Lindblad--Sudarshan (GKLS) master equation. From the time-dependent covariance matrix we extract the quantum Fisher information (QFI) for general single-mode Gaussian probe states, including squeezed ones. In the strong-coupling, non-Markovian regime the QFI is non-monotonic in time, displaying bath-memory revivals that make a finite interrogation time $t^*>0$ strictly optimal. By contrast, we prove that the Markovian QFI rises monotonically to its stationary value and develops no interior optimum, so that its optimum is always pinned to the boundary $t^*\to\infty$; this complements existing Markovian precision-rate bounds, which concern $(\mathcal F(t)/t)$ rather than the single-shot QFI $(\mathcal F(t))$. Squeezed initial states yield a large transient advantage that thermalisation eventually erases, establishing squeezing and interrogation time as complementary thermometric resources. At equilibrium, strong coupling replaces the exponential Boltzmann suppression of the low-temperature relative error by a far milder polynomial divergence. As the model maps directly onto circuit quantum electrodynamics, these protocols appear within current experimental reach.

Abstract: Traditional quantum control relies on an iterative "simulate-then-optimize" paradigm, where dynamics simulation and control design are decoupled, leading to substantial computational overhead and limited scalability, particularly in noisy environments. Here, we propose an end-to-end quantum control framework based on long short-term memory, in which system dynamics and control strategies are learned jointly in a low dimensional latent manifold. The model directly maps initial states and environmental parameters to both dynamical trajectories and optimized control pulse in a single forward pass. The framework is validated on adiabatic speedup in a two-level system and state transfer in a one-dimensional spin chain under noise, achieving accurate dynamical prediction and control optimization. It improves the fidelity for both tasks and significantly reduces the optimization cost by three orders of magnitude compared with conventional iterative methods, while exhibiting strong generalization to multi-parameter, time-varying noise, as well as to different initial states and driving fields. Our work introduces a data-driven control paradigm based on latent manifold learning, reducing the computational bottleneck of iterative optimization and enabling real-time adaptive control of complex open quantum systems.

Abstract: Threshold private set intersection (TPSI) allows parties to reveal their intersection only when its cardinality reaches a prescribed threshold. Existing quantum TPSI protocols typically rely on a third party (TP) to interpret the final results, which deviates from the cardinality-testing paradigm of TPSI. In this paper, we propose a quantum multiparty TPSI protocol with explicit cardinality testing. Our protocol develops a rotation-based quantum construction in which single-photon sequences are sequentially processed through participant-side data rotations, TP--participant masking rotations, and correlated aggregate rotations. This design produces hidden-label measurement vectors: TP can complete the final measurement, but cannot interpret the semantic meaning of the outcomes. Based on these hidden measurements, we further realize the threshold decision through an oblivious linear evaluation (OLE)-based inner product procedure and a lightweight garbled circuit, revealing only \(\mathbf 1[|\bigcap_i X_i|\ge τ]\) before conditional intersection reconstruction. We prove the correctness and security of the proposed protocol, and further validate its feasibility through quantum-circuit simulations implemented on the IBM \textsf{Qiskit} platform.

Conclusion: 硬核玻色子代数在量子电路模拟中具有计算效率优势，并可扩展至量子电路综合任务，展示了该代数框架的实用价值。

Abstract: The use of algebraic frameworks based on complex Clifford algebras for the representation and simulation of quantum circuits has been discussed in the literature. Recently, an alternative algebraic approach employing hard-core bosons has been proposed. Hard-core bosons provide a natural representation of multi-qubit systems, in which the tensor-product structure is realized directly and no sign corrections are required, in contrast to realizations based on complex Clifford algebras. Although both approaches are formally equivalent, the hard-core boson formulation exhibits computational advantages. This work reviews and extends the hard-core boson algebra for circuit simulation and presents an efficient implementation. A performance comparison with IBM Qiskit shows substantially improved execution times for simulations. Moreover, a new application is introduced in which the hard-core boson formalism is combined with genetic algorithms for quantum circuit synthesis.

</details>

### [81] [A Reproducible Pipeline for Symmetry-Respecting Excited States on Near-Term Quantum Computers: The H2O/STO-3G Case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28130)
*Huajing Song*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文以H₂O分子（STO-3G基组，12量子比特）为完整测试系统，系统分析了变分激发态量子算法在贫瘠高原、对称性污染、有限采样不稳定性和硬件成本等多个失败原因上的综合表现。研究发现：裸哈密顿量下阳离子态与中性态交错；硬件高效和数守恒ansätze因Brillouin定理陷入Hartree-Fock不动点，而ADAPT-VQE可逃脱；变分紧缩法继承污染并导致谱反转，而量子运动方程（qEOM）子空间法恢复亚毫哈特里的精度；粒子数在散粒噪声下结构性地受保护；结合矩阵感知的散粒分配，约3×10⁹次总散粒即可达到化学精度，比朴素逐元素估计低三个数量级，可在数天内完成。单电路门保真度而非测量是主要瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分激发态量子算法在多个失效因素（贫瘠高原、对称性污染、有限采样不稳定性、硬件成本）上通常被孤立研究，缺乏将这些因素整合在一个完整系统中进行系统性分析和基准测试的工作。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 以H₂O分子（STO-3G基组，12量子比特，Jordan-Wigner变换）为完整测试系统，构建可复现的流水线，将所有结果与精确对角化进行对比。比较了多种ansätze（硬件高效、数守恒、ADAPT-VQE）和激发态求解方法（变分紧缩法、qEOM子空间法），分析了散粒噪声下的粒子数保护，并引入矩阵感知的散粒分配策略以降低测量成本。

Result: 裸哈密顿量中阳离子态（N=7）与中性态交错；硬件高效和数守恒ansätze在Hartree-Fock处停滞（精确不动点），ADAPT-VQE可逃脱；变分紧缩法继承污染并导致能谱反转，qEOM子空间法恢复亚毫哈特里精度；粒子数在散粒噪声下结构性地受保护；矩阵感知散粒分配使总散粒数降至~3×10⁹（比朴素估计低三个数量级），可在数天内达到化学精度；单电路门保真度是主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: 本文作为一个教学和基准测试参考，系统揭示了多种激发态量子算法失效机制在真实分子系统中的综合表现，强调了qEOM子空间法在激发态计算中的优势，并指出单电路门保真度（而非测量）是当前硬件约束的主要瓶颈。所有代码、参数和图表均已开放。

Abstract: Variational excited-state quantum algorithms fail for reasons usually studied in isolation: barren plateaus, symmetry contamination, finite-sampling instability, and hardware cost. Using one small but complete system -- H$_2$O in the STO-3G basis (12 qubits, Jordan--Wigner) -- we assemble these into a single reproducible pipeline, checking every claim against exact diagonalization. The bare qubit Hamiltonian interleaves cation ($N{=}7$) states below the neutral manifold; hardware-efficient and number-conserving ansätze stall at Hartree--Fock, an exact stationary point by Brillouin's theorem, while ADAPT-VQE escapes; variational deflation inherits the contamination and inverts the spectrum, whereas the quantum equation-of-motion (qEOM) subspace method restores the ladder to sub-milli-Hartree accuracy. Particle number is protected \emph{structurally} under shot noise, and a realistic measurement model collapses the thousands of subspace matrix elements to $\sim\!10^5$ commuting groups; a matrix-aware shot allocation then reaches chemical accuracy at $\sim\!3\times10^9$ total shots -- a thousandfold below the naive per-element estimate and reachable in days -- leaving single-circuit gate fidelity, not measurement, as the binding constraint. This work is a teaching and benchmarking reference, not a new method; all code, parameters, and figures are released.

</details>


### [82] [Optimizing Resource Costs: A Practical Guide to Achieving Target Security in Verifiable Blind Quantum Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28139)
*Janice van Dam,Michał van Hooft,Stephanie D. C. Wehner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文形式化了可验证盲量子计算(VBQC)协议中参数优化为约束优化问题，开发了求解框架以最小化轮数，推导了最小轮数的启发式公式，并通过离子阱服务器案例展示了从硬件规格到协议参数和运行时间的端到端优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Leichtle等人的噪声鲁棒VBQC协议涉及大量相互依赖的参数，在给定硬件噪声水平和安全目标下难以找到有效的参数集。

Method: 将参数选择形式化为约束优化问题，开发求解框架；推导最小轮数的启发式公式以快速估计资源；通过离子阱服务器案例进行验证。

Result: 得到最小化轮数的协议参数；推导出描述轮数与噪声及安全目标标度关系的启发式公式；实现了速率-保真度权衡的端到端运行时间优化。

Conclusion: 该框架能为近期的可验证盲量子计算实现提供具体的参数指导和运行时间估计。

Abstract: Verifiable blind quantum computing (VBQC) enables a resource-limited client to securely delegate computations to an untrusted quantum server while maintaining privacy and detecting deviations from the prescribed computation. The noise-robust VBQC protocol of Leichtle et al. achieves this through a round-based structure: the client delegates multiple computation rounds and test rounds, using the test outcomes to detect cheating while tolerating honest hardware noise. The protocol's security proof involves numerous interdependent parameters, making it non-trivial to find a valid parameter set for a given hardware noise level and security target. We formalize this as a constrained optimization problem and develop a practical framework to solve it. The framework yields the protocol parameters that minimize the number of rounds for any given setup. We derive a heuristic formula for the minimal number of rounds to help understand the scaling with noise and security targets and to provide rapid resource estimation. Since the number of rounds depends on noise while the time per round depends on hardware rate, the framework also enables optimization of rate-fidelity trade-offs to minimize end-to-end runtime. We demonstrate both applications through a case study of a trapped-ion server with a measurement-only client, showing how the client's polarization control hardware specifications translate into protocol parameters and runtime estimates, providing concrete guidance for near-term implementations.

</details>

We show that continuity between the boundaries of timelike and null infinity implies that the late-time limit of the Bondi mass aspect naturally acts as a detector operator for massive outgoing radiation. Finally, we interpret the Bondi mass aspect as a Carrollian stress-tensor component, and study Ward identities to constrain its two-point functions.

### [85] [Soft QED as Open Quantum System: Infrared Cancellation and Soft-Shell Coarse Graining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27498)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将QED系统划分为解析部分（带电粒子和硬光子）与未解析环境（软光子），采用约化密度矩阵和Kraus算符形式。利用Schwinger-Keldysh形式统一处理未解析的虚项和实项，通过等历史恒等式规范软演化，结合软光子定理去除红外发散主导软因子。推导标度参数化的Lindblad演化方程和完全正定Schur通道。

Result: 开放量子系统框架与完整QED在相同可观测量、微扰阶、图和相空间下给出相同的红外有限项。推导了标度参数化的Lindblad演化，得到对角跃迁算符，有限壳映射是完全正定单射Schur通道，在标度不变领先软区域形成完全正定可分流退相半群。预言了对数可见度斜率和单调纯度损失。

Conclusion: 开放量子系统方法有效组织了QED的红外结构，软光子扇区由散射电流驱动的相干态位移统一描述，为处理红外发散和软光子效应提供了系统的理论框架。

Abstract: I formulate unresolved soft-photon sector of QED as open quantum system. Resolved charged particles and hard photons form the system, unresolved soft photons form the environment, and basic object is the reduced density matrix. A resolved outcome $f$ of multiple hard particles and photons has probability $P_{f}(i) =\sum_n|\langle f,n|S|i,0\rangle|^2=\langle i|F_f|i\rangle$, with Kraus operators $K_n= {}_{\rm soft} \langle n|S|0 \rangle_{\rm soft}$ and effect $F_f=\sum_nK_n^\daggerΠ_fK_n$. The SK formulation places unresolved virtual and real terms in one doubled-contour expansion. At one loop they carry the same on-shell eikonal kernel with opposite signs. This elegantly organizes the QED probability: for the same observable, perturbative order, diagrams, and phase space, the OQS gives the same infrared-finite terms as the full-QED. The soft-photon evolution is a unitary coherent-state displacement driven by the scattering current. The equal-history identity of influence functional exactly normalizes this soft evolution; together with the soft-photon theorem it removes the IR divergent leading-soft factor from inclusive probability. I also derive explicit leading-soft QED realization of scale-parametrized Lindblad evolution on a fixed hard-branch space. Tracing an infinitesimal soft-photon shell produces diagonal jump operators whose entries are fixed by the corresponding eikonal emission amplitudes. The finite-shell map is a completely positive unital Schur channel and, in the sharp scale-invariant leading-soft regime, a dephasing semigroup of a completely-positive-divisible scale flow. The resulting logarithmic visibility slope and monotonic purity loss are off-diagonal predictions of the reduced-state description. The same controlled-displacement dilation gives the Sudakov probability, Poisson soft-photon multiplicities, and the bremsstrahlung number spectrum.

The requirement that the orbifolded brane brick model remains consistent with the closed paths associated with the J- and E-terms, together with the chiral cycles formed by their products, precisely reproduces the Calabi-Yau condition on the orbifold action. This procedure yields an explicit formula for the J- and E-terms of the orbifolded brane brick model in terms of those of the parent theory. We apply our construction to the brane brick models corresponding to Q^{1,1,1} and D_3, and present the resulting families of 2d (0,2) quiver gauge theories. *Yilber Fabian Bautista,Mathias Driesse,Kays Haddad,Gustav Uhre Jakobsen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用世界线量子场论形式，计算了引力波与无自旋点粒子散射在牛顿常数四阶下的振幅。通过引入Murua系数的积分分解方法，避免了散射振幅到Magnusian转换中的切割减法，并将结果与黑洞微扰理论匹配，证明了世界线量子场论能准确描述至G⁴阶的Schwarzschild黑洞。此过程中椭圆函数首次出现在动量空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算引力波与点粒子散射在牛顿常数四阶（G⁴）下的振幅，并验证世界线量子场论能否准确描述Schwarzschild黑洞的散射行为。

Method: 采用世界线量子场论形式，利用Murua系数分解主积分，避免切割减法；将结果与黑洞微扰理论匹配。

Result: 成功计算了G⁴阶散射振幅，证明了点粒子世界线量子场论能准确描述Schwarzschild黑洞；椭圆函数首次在该过程的动量空间中出现。

Conclusion: 世界线量子场论可精确描述Schwarzschild黑洞的引力波散射至G⁴阶，且椭圆函数在动量空间的出现为该过程的新特征。

Abstract: We compute the amplitude for the scattering of a gravitational wave off of a spinless point particle at fourth order in Newton's constant, using the worldline quantum field theory formalism. A decomposition of our master integrals incorporating Murua coefficients allows us to entirely bypass the cut subtraction needed to convert the scattering amplitude into the Magnusian, the latter being desirable as it maps directly onto the scattering phase shift in partial wave space. This is then matched to the prediction from black hole perturbation theory, proving that point-particle worldline quantum field theory accurately describes Schwarzschild black holes up to $\mathcal{O}(G^4)$. Elliptic functions appear in momentum space for the first time for this process at this order.

</details>

Abstract: We review the representations of so(1,D), the algebra of isometries of D dimensional de Sitter space. We cover the representations in all D, including mixed symmetry representations and fermionic representations, and connect them to the various types of fields that can propagate on de Sitter space. The presentation is from a physics point of view, favoring concrete constructions over abstract considerations.

### [89] [CIPro Package: Complete Intersections in Products of Projective Spaces and Line Bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27588)

Abstract: CIPro is a Mathematica package for constructing and analyzing complete intersections in products of projective spaces and line bundles over such varieties. It computes properties of complete intersections, such as Chern classes, Hilbert series, GV invariants and symmetries, as well as properties of line bundles on complete intersections, including their cohomology groups. The package also consolidates a number of data sets available in the literature into a single system, including the lists of complete intersection Calabi-Yau three- and four-folds. This short tutorial introduces the package, provides a brief discussion of some of the mathematical background underlying its computations, and gives a series of examples to illustrate its use. These tools are of utility for many computations in string compactifications, especially for Calabi-Yau geometries appearing in Heterotic and Type II constructions. Many tools apply beyond the Calabi-Yau context, including for example, almost Fano bases in F-theory.

### [90] [Classification of Killing Horizons in D=11 Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27843)
*Jan Gutowski,Chettha Saelim,Martin Wolf*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在D=11超引力中，对远离近极端极限的、具有闭空间截面的超对称退化Killing视界进行分类。证明所有此类解分为两类：第一类中，Killing旋子的负光锥手征部分在视界上非零，此类解等距于超对称近极端几何；第二类中，该部分在视界上为零，此时Killing旋子对生成视界的Killing矢量的旋量李导数为零，且具有超过13个超对称性的解为pp波。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Gaussian零坐标系的类光手征性分析，将Killing旋子按负光锥手征部分是否为零分为两类，分别证明其几何性质。

Result: 所有解分为两类：第一类等距于超对称近极端几何；第二类中旋量李导数为零，且超过13个超对称性时解为pp波。

Conclusion: 建立了D=11超引力中超对称退化Killing视界的完整分类，揭示了类光手征性在决定视界几何结构中的关键作用。

Abstract: We initiate the classification of supersymmetric degenerate Killing horizons, with closed spatial cross section, away from the near-horizon limit in D=11 supergravity. We prove that all such solutions fall into two distinct classes, depending on lightcone chirality with respect to a Gaussian null coordinate system. For the first class of solutions, the negative lightcone chirality part of the Killing spinor is non-zero on the Killing horizon, and we prove that all such solutions are isometric to supersymmetric near-horizon geometries. In the second class, the negative lightcone chirality part of the Killing spinor vanishes on the Killing horizon. In this case, we prove that the spinorial Lie derivative of the Killing spinor with respect to the Killing vector which generates the Killing horizon vanishes, and that all such solutions with more than 13 supersymmetries are pp-waves.

</details>

Result: 对于0≤λ<1，非弹性散射过程发生非平凡抵消，使得世界片散射保持可积性；λ→1时S矩阵变得病态，该极限无法完全捕捉T-对偶理论的世界片动力学。

For generic values of $0 \leq λ< 1$, we show that the worldsheet scattering remains compatible with integrability due to a non-trivial cancellation of non-elastic scattering processes. By contrast, the S matrix becomes ill-defined for $λ\to 1$, despite the fact that this limit reproduces the non-Abelian T-dual geometry up to an analytic continuation. This suggests that the $λ\to 1$ limit does not capture the full worldsheet dynamics of the T-dual theory.

### [92] [Higher dimensional quantum Hall effect and the analog of $W_\infty$-algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28219)
*Dimitra Karabali,V. P. Nair*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明阿贝尔和非阿贝尔规范变换是高维量子霍尔效应中W_∞变换的类比。通过纯粹拓扑论证，利用反常下降程序中的双上循环及体-边作用量之间的反常抵消，得到了边缘模上这类变换的对易子反常和扩展代数。该方法依赖Dolbeault指标定理构造体作用量，所得代数与现有边缘模计算结果一致，并比较了二维与高维中这些变换的异同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用反常下降程序中的双上循环和体-边界反常抵消机制，结合Dolbeault指标定理构造体作用量，通过纯拓扑论证推导边缘模上的变换代数。

Result: 证明了高维中规范变换等价于W_∞变换，推导出了边缘模上的扩展代数，与现有边缘模计算结果一致。

Conclusion: 规范变换与W_∞变换在高维量子霍尔效应中本质相同，拓扑方法可统一处理不同维度的边缘模代数结构，并指出了二维与高维之间的异同。

Abstract: We show that Abelian and nonabelian gauge transformations are the analog of $W_\infty$ transformations for higher dimensional quantum Hall effect. The commutator anomaly and the extended algebra of such transformations on the edge modes of a droplet are obtained by purely topological arguments, basically utilizing the two-cocycle in the descent procedure for anomalies and using the fact that there is anomaly cancellation between the bulk and boundary actions. The method relies on the fact that bulk actions are easily constructed in general using the Dolbeault index theorem. The resulting algebras are shown to agree with explicit edge mode calculations for cases where they are available. We also comment on the similarities and differences in the nature of these transformations between two and higher dimensions.

### [93] [A UV-Finite Ryu-Takayanagi Relation from Relative Entropy in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27915)
*Albert Much,Philipp Dorau,Leonardo Sangaletti,Rainer Verch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在AdS₃/CFT₂中利用相对熵（替代紫外发散的冯·诺依曼纠缠熵）建立了Ryu-Takayanagi关系。通过将手征相对熵精确结果推广到菱形区域，将真空与相干态间的边界相对熵表示为Schwarzian泛函，Fefferman-Graham字典将其识别为Bañados几何的渐近数据；三维引力的刚性将该边界识别提升到体时空。在线性阶，相对熵等于RT测地线长度变化除以4G_N。该构造仅依赖Bisognano-Wichmann/Borchers定理与全息字典，给出了RT关系的紫外有限、算子代数对应物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立一种紫外有限的Ryu-Takayanagi关系，避免使用传统纠缠熵中出现的紫外发散，从而从算子代数角度为全息纠缠熵提供更严格的数学基础。

Method: 将Hollands关于手征相对熵的精确结果推广到菱形区域；利用Fefferman-Graham字典将边界相对熵识别为Bañados几何的渐近数据；借助三维引力的刚性将边界识别推广到体时空；线性化近似下计算相对熵与RT测地线长度的关系。

Result: 在线性阶，相对熵等于RT测地线长度变化除以4G_N，建立了紫外有限的RT关系。

Conclusion: 本文给出了RT关系的紫外有限、算子代数对应物，不依赖于紫外截断，仅基于Bisognano-Wichmann/Borchers定理和全息字典，为全息纠缠熵提供了更坚实的数学基础。

Abstract: We establish a Ryu-Takayanagi (RT) relation in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ using \emph{relative entropy} as the central object, in place of the ultraviolet-divergent von Neumann entanglement entropy. Adapting Hollands' exact result for the chiral relative entropy to a diamond region, we express the boundary relative entropy between the vacuum and a coherent state as a Schwarzian functional, which the Fefferman-Graham dictionary identifies with the asymptotic data of a Bañados geometry; the rigidity of three-dimensional gravity promotes this boundary identification to the bulk. To linear order in the metric perturbation, the relative entropy then equals the variation of the RT geodesic length divided by $4G_N$. The construction rests only on the Bisognano-Wichmann/Borchers theorem and the holographic dictionary, giving a UV-finite, operator-algebraic counterpart to the RT relation.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现相图与一维量子球形p自旋模型定性相似，存在低温自旋玻璃相，该相具有有限的爱德华-安德森序参数，双点函数动力学部分展示近似标度行为。

Conclusion: 该模型为研究二维无序相对论性场论中的近似共形行为和玻璃态物理提供了一个可处理的平台。

Abstract: We introduce a two-dimensional $O(N)$ nonlinear sigma model with random Gaussian $p$-body interactions. The model combines the structure of a two-dimensional bosonic SYK-type quantum field theory with the stabilizing spherical constraint of the nonlinear sigma model. At large $N$ we derive the Schwinger-Dyson equations on a torus and analyze the solutions using both analytical approximations and numerical methods. We find a phase diagram qualitatively similar to that of the one-dimensional quantum spherical $p$-spin model, including a low-temperature transition to a spin glass phase. This phase is characterized by a finite Edwards-Anderson order parameter, while the dynamical part of the two-point function displays an approximate scaling regime. These results provide a tractable setting for studying approximate conformal behavior and glassy physics in a two-dimensional relativistic field theory with disorder.

### [95] [$\texttt{SMaSH}$ : Simplify Massive Spinor Helicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27928)
*Aakash Kumar,Arnab Rudra,Rahul Shaw*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文介绍了SMaSH，一个用于四维时空自旋螺旋度计算的Mathematica软件包，支持有质量自旋螺旋度计算（含显式小群指标）、无质量和离壳自旋螺旋度变量，可实现微扰计算、高能极限、C/P/T变换检查、接触项计算和规范不变性验证，并能通过RAMBO算法生成任意n点散射的数值运动学。该软件包还包含基本的自旋螺旋度操作功能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该软件包能够成功计算规范不变的Weinberg最小振幅（arXiv:2506:12431, arXiv:2504:06343），支持任意n点散射的实数和复数数值运动学生成，并实现了完整的自旋螺旋度代数操作。

Conclusion: SMaSH填补了有质量自旋螺旋度计算工具的空缺，为高能物理微扰计算提供了一个功能全面、易于使用的Mathematica软件包。

Abstract: We present $\texttt{SMaSH}$, a $\texttt{Mathematica}$ package to do spinor helicity computations in four spacetime dimensions $\href{https://github.com/aakash-kmr/SMaSH}{\text{(github)}}$. It can handle massive spinor helicity computations with explicit little group indices which is a novel feature. It can also handle massless as well as off-shell spinor helicity variables. It is designed to compute perturbative computations; it comes with predefined three point amplitudes and propagators for any masses and spins (arXiv:1709.04891). It can implement the high energy limit over an expression, check the discrete $\tt{C,P,T}$ transformations, compute contact terms and impose gauge invariance for any scattering process. We have shown the usage of such functions for computing gauge invariant Weinberg minimal amplitudes (arXiv:2506:12431, arXiv:2504:06343).
  The package can also generate both real and complex numerical kinematics for any $n$-point scattering for arbitrary masses and energy scales by implementing the $\tt{RAMBO}$ algorithm. It is also rich with basic spinor helicity manipulations like Schouten simplification, Clifford algebra manipulation, conversion between spinor helicity and Lorentz vectors, derivative w.r.t. spinors and their scalars, helicity scaling etc.

### [96] [Quantum black hole cohomologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27955)
*Seok Kim,Seongmin Kim,Siyul Lee,Jiyoo Park*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究BPS AdS黑洞微态在超杨-米尔斯理论中的量子修正问题，发现在SO(7)和SU(2)理论中，经典黑洞（偶然）上同调会被1圈修正 lifted，但最轻的偶然上同调及其“毛状”版本未被 lifted，而许多更重的“核心”偶然上同调被 lifted。经典上同调的熵在Cardy极限下比严格保护态的指标熵至少大1.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BPS AdS黑洞微态可以从经典超杨-米尔斯理论的上同调研究，但其量子性质一直是推测性的。作者旨在探究量子修正（尤其是1圈修正）如何影响这些经典上同调，以理解黑洞微态的量子本质。

Method: 通过在SU(2)超杨-米尔斯理论中计算1圈修正对经典偶然上同调的影响，对比SO(7)理论中已有的结果，区分被 lifted 和未被 lifted 的上同调类型，并在Cardy极限下计算和比较经典上同调熵与严格保护态指标熵。

Result: 在SU(2)理论中，1圈修正会提升（lift）部分经典偶然上同调而保持其他不变。具体而言，最轻的偶然上同调及其“毛状”版本未被 lifted，而更重的“核心”偶然上同调大多被 lifted。经典上同调的熵在Cardy极限下比严格保护态的指标熵至少大1.2%。

Conclusion: 量子修正对经典黑洞上同调有选择性提升效应，并非所有经典上同调都能存活到量子层面。这暗示BPS黑洞微态的量子描述比经典图像更为精细，需要区分不同性质的微态贡献。

Abstract: Microstates of BPS AdS black holes have been studied from the classical cohomologies of the maximal super-Yang-Mills theories, but their quantum natures have been conjectural. It was recently found that a classical black hole (fortuitous) cohomology in the $SO(7)$ theory is lifted by 1-loop corrections. We show that such lifts also happen in the $SU(2)$ theory, presenting both lifted/unlifted examples. In particular, the lightest fortuitous cohomology and its `hairy' versions are unlifted, while many heavier `core' fortuitous ones are lifted. We argue that the entropy of classical cohomologies in the Cardy limit is larger than the indicial entropy of strictly protected states by at least $\approx 1.2 \%$.

### [97] [Non-primary square roots in massive gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28208)
*Alexey Golovnev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文指出非主平方根在适当理解下同样满足一般协变性，但其真正问题在于微扰理论中不存在相应矩阵表示，且拉格朗日密度中的初等对称多项式不解析，非主平方根更易进入复数域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对文献中声称非主平方根会破坏一般协变性、应使用主平方根的观点，作者试图证明非主平方根在正确理解下也是协变的，同时指出其真正问题在于微扰理论和非解析性。

Method: 从矩阵分析和拉格朗日密度中的初等对称多项式两个角度，分析非主平方根在dRGT巨引力和双度量引力中的协变性、微扰存在性及解析性。

Result: 非主平方根在适当意义下满足一般协变性；但在微扰理论中矩阵平方根本身不存在，且初等对称多项式不解析；非主平方根更容易进入复数域。

Conclusion: 反对非主平方根应基于微扰理论和非解析性等实质问题，而非协变性，后者在正确理解下仍然成立。

Abstract: Non-linear dRGT massive and bimetric gravities are complicated theories constructed in terms of square roots of matrices. Apart from the technical issues of successfully working with such square roots, there is also a problem of their non-uniqueness. There are claims in the literature that one should better use the principal root. This is a very reasonable conclusion. However, the motivation they give for it is that otherwise there would be non-primary square roots violating the general covariance. In this paper, I would like to show that, if properly understood, the non-primary square roots are also perfectly covariant. At the same time, I recall the relatively old observation that the real problem with such square roots lies in perturbation theory around them. In terms of matrices, it simply does not exist. In terms of the elementary symmetric polynomials used in the Lagrangian density, it is not analytic. Moreover, the non-principal square roots are more prone to getting into the complex domain.

</details>


### [98] [Planar loop integrands from cuts in $D$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28052)
*Fan Zhu,Song He,Zhenqi Han*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从D维广义幺正割直接重构平面圈被积函数的公式，适用于任意带色理论。该方法将重构组合学与树图振幅分离，通过Möbius逆变换或欧拉示性数给出系数，并在纯杨-米尔斯理论、最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论中得到验证与应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有圈被积函数重构方法依赖特定理论或维度，缺乏普适的、与树图振幅解耦的组合重构公式，且在高圈多点情形下计算复杂。

Method: 将被积函数表示为可容许非无标量标量图的加权和，系数由精化偏序集的Möbius逆变换（或关联复形的欧拉示性数）给出；割由胶合D维树图振幅并求和内禀胶子态生成。

Result: 在纯杨-米尔斯理论中给出闭式公式；通过二圈五点验证了与已知被积函数及积分后螺旋度振幅的一致性；给出了二圈六点、三圈四点等更大案例的紧致割组织化数据；描述了最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论中因无泡泡和三角形子图导致的割偏序集简化。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种系统化、普适的圈被积函数重构方案，分离了组合结构与动力学内容，适用于任意圈数和点数的带色理论，并能自然推广到超对称情形。

Abstract: We present a direct reconstruction formula for planar loop integrands from $D$-dimensional generalized unitarity cuts in any colored theory. The reconstruction combinatorics is separated from the theory-dependent tree amplitudes entering the cuts: for the $L$-loop $n$-point color-ordered amplitude, the integrand is expressed as a sum over admissible non-scaleless scalar graphs dressed by corresponding cuts in $D$ dimensions; the coefficients are given by the universal Möbius-inversion formula of the refinement poset, or equivalently one minus the Euler characteristics of associated complexes.
  As an application we write down closed-formulas for loop integrands in pure Yang--Mills theory, where the required cuts are generated by gluing $D$-dimensional tree amplitudes and summing over internal gluon states. We also use the two-loop five-point case as a validation, comparing with known integrand data and after integration-by-parts reduction, with known integrated helicity amplitudes. The same framework also produces compact cut-organized data for larger examples, including the two-loop six-point and three-loop four-point cases. We also describe the corresponding simplification in maximally supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory, where the absence of bubble and triangle subgraphs reduces the relevant cut poset substantially.

### [99] [New Solutions of RG Equations for α_s and y_{top}](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28084)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造了重整化群(RG)方程的简单解析解，解的形式仅包含对数函数，无需特殊函数，能够系统地求和领头阶、次领头阶等对数项。

Result: y_{top}对α_s跑动的影响可忽略不计；α_s对y_{top}跑动的影响至关重要；考虑高阶修正后，对y_{top}跑动的贡献显著增加。

Conclusion: 所构建的解析解有效地描述了渐近区域中耦合常数的跑动行为，揭示了α_s与y_{top}之间不对称的相互影响关系，表明在精确计算y_{top}跑动时必须考虑α_s的高阶修正效应。

Abstract: We construct simple analytical solutions of the RG equations for the running couplings α_s and y_{top} in the asymptotic regime. These solutions have an explicit form, contain only logarithms and no special functions, and subsequently sum up the leading, subleading, etc logarithms in all orders of PT. While the effect of y_{top} on the running of α_s happens to be negligible, the role of α_s on the running of y_{top} is essential, the account of higher orders gives a noticeable contribution.

### [100] [Configurational Temperature in Matrix Models and Random Matrix Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28148)
*Anosh Joseph,Vinod Mamale*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究相互作用矩阵模型和高斯随机矩阵系综中的构形温度估计量，该估计量源自精确的Schwinger-Dyson恒等式，可用作用量的梯度和Hessian矩阵表示。在Gross-Witten-Wadia模型、四势阱双阱矩阵模型以及高斯正交/幺正/辛系综中，估计量均满足β_config=1的精确Schwinger-Dyson恒等式。将估计量分解为各向同性和各向异性部分后，发现主导的有限N修正满足β_iso - 1 ≃ -β_aniso的近似关系。同时证明构形温度估计量是蒙特卡罗模拟的灵敏诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Schwinger-Dyson恒等式推导构形温度估计量，将其分解为各向同性和各向异性部分；在多种矩阵模型（GWW模型、双阱矩阵模型、GOE/GUE/GSE）中进行数值模拟，分析统计不确定度下的行为及有限N修正。

Result: 所有模型中β_config=1在统计不确定度内成立；各向同性与各向异性部分的主导有限N修正满足β_iso - 1 ≃ -β_aniso的近似关系；构形温度估计量可作为MC模拟的有效诊断工具。

Conclusion: 构形温度估计量在矩阵模型中可靠地满足精确Schwinger-Dyson恒等式，其分解形式揭示了有限N修正的对称性关系，且在数值模拟诊断中具有高灵敏度。

Abstract: We investigate the configurational temperature estimator in interacting matrix models and Gaussian random-matrix ensembles. The estimator follows from an exact Schwinger--Dyson identity and may be expressed in terms of the gradient and Hessian of the action. We study the Gross--Witten--Wadia model, a quartic double-well matrix model, and the Gaussian Orthogonal, Unitary, and Symplectic Ensembles. In all cases, the estimator satisfies the exact Schwinger--Dyson identity, $β_{\rm config} = 1$, within statistical uncertainties. Separating the estimator into isotropic and anisotropic parts, we find that the leading finite-$N$ corrections satisfy the approximate relation $β_{\rm iso} - 1 \simeq - β_{\rm aniso}$. We also show that the configurational temperature estimator provides a sensitive diagnostic of Monte Carlo simulations.

Conclusion: 该研究为微扰量子引力中视界的规范不变量子涨落可在远大于普朗克尺度的尺度上存在提供了最严格的证据。

Abstract: We study the quantum fluctuations of the black hole horizon in three-dimensional Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime. We define a precise protocol to calculate the horizon fluctuations and define a corresponding ``quantum width'' of the horizon. We relate the horizon fluctuations to boundary correlation functions via holography. Working in perturbative quantum gravity, we find that the quantum width is typically of order $(G_\mathrm{N} L_{\mathrm{AdS}}^3 )^{1/4}$, which is parametrically larger than the Planck scale. In detail, the quantum width depends on the scale at which it is measured, diverging logarithmically in the UV. Our results give the most rigorous evidence to date of gauge-invariant fluctuations at scales much larger than the Planck scale within perturbative quantum gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三点在壳振幅技术，利用无质量螺旋旋量作为基本构建块，引入离散C、P、T变换的在壳表示。方法的核心输入是局部或整体的经典对称性（可能被反常破坏）以及有效作用量的对称性，但不依赖有效作用量的显式形式。通过对称性约束在壳振幅，推导反常结构。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种纯粹基于在壳技术的反常分析方法，为理解和计算量子反常提供了新的、简洁的理论框架，避免了传统路径积分或图方法的复杂性。

Abstract: We bootstrap quantum anomalies using on-shell techniques in the simplest setting: at three points. The necessary field-theoretic input includes the local or global classical symmetry, which the anomaly may break, and the symmetries of the effective action -- though not its explicit form. We use massless helicity spinors together with an on-shell representation of the discrete C, P, and T transformations. Our approach determines the Weyl, chiral (global and local), diffeomorphism, and Lorentz anomalies up to real constant prefactors. In particular, we recover gauge-anomaly cancelation conditions, as well as find that the Weyl anomaly should not involve Pontryagin densities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用可积sigma模型的单值矩阵形式，利用幂零代数结构的性质实现单值矩阵的显式因子化，并通过引入多极点将构造推广至多中心构型。

Abstract: We construct a new class of exact solutions describing multi-black holes in the Bertotti--Robinson spacetime, using the monodromy-matrix formalism associated with integrable sigma models. Starting from the extremal Reissner--Nordström black hole in the Bertotti--Robinson background, we derive the corresponding coset and monodromy matrices and show that they are governed by nilpotent algebraic structures. This property enables an explicit factorization of the monodromy matrix, allowing for a systematic reconstruction of the underlying gravitational solutions. We extend this construction to multi-center configurations by introducing multiple poles in the monodromy matrix, leading to Majumdar--Papapetrou--type solutions with Bertotti--Robinson asymptotics. Each center is shown to correspond to a regular extremal black hole with an $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times S^2$ near-horizon geometry, and the asymptotic end likewise approaches a Bertotti--Robinson geometry. We further generalize the framework to stationary configurations in the Bertotti--Robinson spacetime, as well as to a broader class of Israel--Wilson--Perjés-type solutions, by considering more general nilpotent elements. Our results demonstrate that the monodromy-matrix approach provides a powerful and systematic framework for constructing multi-black hole solutions in nontrivial backgrounds, and suggest a promising route toward more general configurations.

Abstract: Classical black holes have sharply defined event horizons, but quantum mechanically the horizon acquires a quantum uncertainty, called the `quantum width' by Marolf. We propose a definition of the quantum width by a physical experiment involving the last moment a signal emitted from an ingoing light ray can escape to infinity. Calculations of this observable for spherically symmetric black holes in perturbative quantum gravity reveal that the quantum width depends on the resolution of the probe, and is often much larger than the Planck scale. For example, for Schwarzschild black holes in four dimensions in a particular regime of parameters, a piece of the horizon of size $σ_\perp$ has quantum width roughly $\sqrt{l_P r_s^2/σ_\perp}$.

Result: 成功构建了类似于无质量旋量-螺旋度方法的CSP振幅公式；发现CSP振幅可视为有质量粒子振幅的无限自旋极限；观察到与黑洞散射类似的指数化普适因子；在自对偶理论中发现非平凡的CSP共线振幅，其共线分数由CSP的维度参数约束。

Conclusion: 所提出的新形式为CSP振幅计算提供了简洁有效的工具，揭示了CSP与有质量粒子及黑洞散射之间的深层联系，并指出共线振幅中维度参数的关键约束作用。

Abstract: We propose a new formulation of continuous-spin particles (CSP) with the help of a single two-component spinor to build asymptotic states. This formulation allows to write down amplitudes in a straightforward way, similar to the massless spinor-helicity approach. The helicity states naturally emerge upon decomposing into components of a fixed homogeneity degree. We show that CSP amplitudes can be understood as the infinite-spin limit of amplitudes of massive particles and, similarly to the scattering of black holes, a certain universal factor exponentiates. In analogy with the recent discovery of collinear amplitudes in self-dual theories, we find nontrivial CSP collinear amplitudes where the collinear fractions are constrained by the dimensionful parameter characterising the various continuous-spin particles.

</details>


### [107] [The cosmology of long range Yukawa interactions in general backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28246)
*Guillem Dom`enech,Panagiotis Giannadakis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了早期宇宙中与轻标量场耦合的费米子，在常状态方程宇宙学背景下的行为，发现了两种主要演化机制：标量场在费米子质量消失点附近振荡的标度 regime，以及场趋向于费米子恢复裸质量的渐近 regime，并揭示了标度 regime 源于作用量的近似标度不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙中的长程力可能导致早期结构形成甚至原初黑洞，此前对费米子与轻标量场耦合的研究需要推广到更一般的情形，以理解不同宇宙学背景下的非线性动力学。

Method: 通过考虑一般标量场依赖的耦合，在常状态方程宇宙学背景下进行分析，识别标度 regime 和渐近 regime 两种演化模式，并利用作用量的近似标度（共形）不变性解释标度 regime 的起源。

Result: 发现了两种演化 regime：标度 regime（标量场振荡，费米子能量密度与标量场能量密度之比近似恒定）和渐近 regime（场演化至费米子恢复裸质量）。标度 regime 源于近似标度不变性，并在晚期表现为近似共形不变性。

Conclusion: 该工作为系统研究该系统内扰动增长提供了第一步，有助于理解早期宇宙结构形成和原初黑洞的产生机制。

Abstract: Long-range forces in the early universe may lead to early structure formation and, perhaps, to primordial black holes. We generalise previous studies of fermions coupled to a light scalar field by considering general scalar-field-dependent couplings in cosmological backgrounds with a constant equation of state. We identify two broad regimes: a scaling regime, in which the scalar field oscillates around a point of vanishing fermion mass, and an asymptotic regime, in which the field evolves toward configurations where the fermions recover their bare mass. We show that the scaling regime arises from an approximate scale invariance in the scalar-fermion action, which becomes an approximate conformal invariance at late times. In the scaling regime, the ratio between the scalar and fermion energy densities is approximately constant. Our work provides a first step toward a general study of the growth of perturbations in this system.

</details>


### [108] [Surface Water Wave Scattering and the Hydrotope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28280)
*Nima Arkani-Hamed,Francesco Calisto,Nail Ussembayev,W. Wayne Zhao,Zihan Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用高能物理方法研究深水表面重力波的经典树级散射振幅。在一维水平散射和两负波数扇区中，得到了n波散射的封闭公式。除运动学前因子外，振幅是经典多面体（被超平面切割的盒子，称为"hydrotope"）的体积，其作用是组织两负波数空间中不同"室"的符号模式。该公式由Claude Opus 4.6在作者指导下发现，基于作者先前在"最简"运动学室中发现的单表达式。结果解决了Y.V. Lvov 1997年五波振幅计算中提出的谜题，将其统一并推广到所有多重性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Y.V. Lvov在1997年五波振幅计算中遗留的谜题，并将计算统一推广到任意多重性。利用高能物理中的散射振幅方法（如多面体体积公式）来研究经典流体力学中的表面重力波散射问题。

Method: 采用高能物理中的树级散射振幅方法，分析一维水平方向上的深水表面重力波散射。聚焦于两负波数扇区，通过识别运动学空间中的"室"结构，将散射振幅表达为"hydrotope"（被超平面切割的盒子）的体积。利用Claude Opus 4.6在作者指导下发现的通用公式，将此前仅在"最简"运动学室中成立的单表达式推广到所有区域。

Result: 得到了n波散射的封闭公式，散射振幅（扣除运动学前因子后）等价于一个经典多面体——hydrotope的体积。该多面体本质上是被超平面切割的盒子，其结构对应于两负波数运动学空间中不同"室"的符号模式。该结果统一并推广了Lvov 1997年的五波计算结果至所有多重性。

Conclusion: 本文展现了高能物理方法（散射振幅、多面体体积）在经典流体力学（表面重力波）中的成功应用，揭示了深水表面重力波散射振幅与经典多面体几何之间的深刻联系，解决了长期悬而未决的谜题，并为该领域的进一步研究提供了通用框架。

Abstract: We study the classical tree-level scattering amplitudes of deep-water surface gravity waves using the methods of high-energy physics. For scattering in one horizontal dimension and in the two-negative-wavenumber sector we obtain a closed formula for $n$-wave scattering. Up to a kinematic prefactor, the amplitude is the volume of a classic polytope -- a box sliced by a hyperplane, which we dub the hydrotope, whose purpose in life is simply to organize the sign patterns of the "chambers" characterizing all the different regions of the two-minus kinematic space. The general formula was discovered by Claude Opus 4.6 working under our guidance, beginning with our earlier discovery of a one-term expression valid in the "simplest" kinematic chamber. Our results resolve the puzzle raised by Y.V. Lvov's 1997 computation of the five-wave amplitudes, unifying and extending it to all multiplicities.

</details>

Abstract: Recent progress on the structure of the quantum connection for monotone symplectic manifolds has used two approaches, which share the common feature of reducing to mod $p$ coefficients. ### [110] [Any-dimensional Positivstellensätze for symmetric functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27551)
*Sebastian Debus,Robin Schabert*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了两个适用于一致正下有界对称函数的Positivstellensätze，并给出了已有归一化对称函数Positivstellensätze的替代证明。

For instance, the underlying domain is not semialgebraic. In this paper, we prove two Positivstellensätze for symmetric functions that are uniformly bounded below by some $\varepsilon > 0$. These are infinite dimensional analogous of theorems of Pólya and Reznick. The proof relates evaluations of the (truncated) power sum map $(p_2,p_3,\dots)$ to moments of discrete probability measures on the compact interval $[-1,1]$. Conclusion: 切丛外幂的Ulrich性质对簇的几何有强约束，分类结果揭示了该条件下Picard数为一的簇的稀少性。

Abstract: We study smooth polarized projective varieties $(X,H)$ whose exterior powers of the tangent bundle are Ulrich. ### [113] [Curves in High Degree Plane Pencils with Bounded Degree Components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27890)
*Hasan Suluyer*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究大次数d的平面曲线束（带有简单基点）中，不可约分支次数不超过k≥2的可约曲线。通过代数几何与组合学技术，建立了此类曲线数量m_k的显式上界，证明对于足够大的d，存在多于六条此类曲线的曲线束不存在。在更强假设d≥(7/2)k(k-1)-2下，得到m_k≤6，改进了此前d≥2k时的已知界。同时给出了含有一条k次不可约分支与直线构成的可约曲线的曲线束的限制条件，并得到某些此类曲线束的不存在性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大次数平面曲线束中可约曲线的数量上界问题，旨在改进已知的数值界，并探索代数几何与组合学方法在此类计数问题中的应用。

Method: 结合代数几何与组合学技术，对带有简单基点的大次数d平面曲线束进行分析，通过建立显式上界并讨论特殊结构（含有一条k次不可约分支与直线的可约曲线）来推导限制条件。

Result: 对于足够大的d，证明了m_k≤6；在d≥(7/2)k(k-1)-2条件下，m_k≤6，改进了此前d≥2k时的结果。同时给出了含特定结构可约曲线的曲线束的限制与不存在性结论。

Conclusion: 大次数平面曲线束中可约曲线的数量存在严格上界（最多6条），进一步的条件可排除某些特殊类型的曲线束存在。

Abstract: In this paper, we study pencils of plane curves of sufficiently large degree $d$ with simple base points, and their reducible curves whose irreducible components have degree at most $k\geq 2$. Combining techniques from algebraic geometry and combinatorics, we establish an explicit upper bound on the number $m_k$ of such curves in the pencils. We prove that, for sufficiently large $d$, pencils with more than six such curves do not exist. Consequently, under the stronger assumption $d\geq\frac{7}{2}k(k-1)-2$, we obtain the bound $m_k\leq 6$, improving the previously known bound for $d \ge 2k$. We also establish restrictions on pencils containing reducible curves consisting of one irreducible component of degree $k$ together with lines, and obtain nonexistence results for certain such pencils.

Abstract: We study the maximal variation problem for linear systems associated with a very ample line bundle, using Hodge theory and Picard-Lefschetz theory. In this note, we generalize this result to Severi--Brauer surfaces over arbitrary ground fields. Using Galois descent, intersection theory and combinatorial arguments, we provide explicit arithmetic and geometric conditions on the centre of the blowing-up.

### [116] [Machine learning fully hadronic events with spectral functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27420)
*Mohammad Mahdi Altakach,Hadi Hassan,Sabine Kraml,Kazuki Sakurai,Haitham Zaraket*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出使用两点关联谱函数作为机器学习输入特征，以解决强子对撞机中全强子事件因QCD辐射导致喷注重数波动的问题。在胶子对产生（$\tilde{g} \to t \bar{t} \tilde{\chi}_1^0$）与全强子$t\bar{t}$本底区分任务中，使用谱函数特征的神经网络相比ATLAS分析将胶子质量灵敏度提升约150 GeV，相比仅用喷注运动学特征的神经网络提升约250 GeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强子对撞机中全强子事件分析面临两大挑战：硬过程信号喷注与初态/末态辐射喷注混杂导致的大组合本底，以及喷注重数在不同事件间涨落导致固定维度输入特征难以适配。现有机器学习方法难以直接处理可变喷注重数问题。

Method: 将事件的横动量数据通过两点关联谱函数映射为角度距离的一维函数，该表示对碰撞器等距变换和喷注排列不敏感，且独立于喷注重数。以谱函数作为输入特征，训练稠密神经网络进行信号-本底分类。

Result: 在139 fb⁻¹的13 TeV pp对撞数据模拟中，谱函数特征神经网络将胶子质量可达灵敏度比ATLAS分析提升约150 GeV，比仅用喷注运动学特征的同网络提升约250 GeV。

Conclusion: 谱函数作为对喷注重数不变的全局事件表示，能有效编码全强子事件的物理信息，显著提升新物理搜索灵敏度。该方法可推广到其他涉及可变喷注重数的强子对撞机分析场景。

Abstract: Characterising fully hadronic events is a difficult task at hadron colliders. Signal jets from the hard process are mingled with an arbitrary number of ISR and FSR jets, leading to a large combinatorial background. This also poses a challenge for machine-learning analyses, where the number of input features is fixed while the jet multiplicity fluctuates from event to event due to QCD radiation. In this work, we explore the use of the two-point correlation spectral function as an input feature for machine-learning analyses of such events. The spectral function maps the transverse-momentum data of an event into a one-dimensional function of the angular distance, encoding the event information modulo collider isometries and jet permutations, and is defined independently of the jet multiplicity. As a concrete benchmark we apply the method to discriminate gluino-pair production followed by $\tilde{g} \to t \bar{t} \tildeχ_1^0$ against the fully hadronic $t \bar{t}$ background. With $139~{\rm fb}^{-1}$ of $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV $pp$ collision data, a dense neural network supplied with spectral-function features improves the expected reach in gluino-mass by roughly 150 GeV relative to a recent ATLAS analysis, and by roughly 250 GeV relative to the same network trained on jet kinematics alone.

</details>


### [117] [Collider Probes of Dark Energy Microphysics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27441)
*Chaitanya Bashyam,Alfredo Gurrola,Andres Florez,Cristian Rodriguez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用高能对撞机（如LHC）测量超出标准模型（BSM）的介质子共振特征来探测暗能量的微观物理，特别是暗能量扰动的声速，建立了一个连接微观与宇宙学尺度的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗能量的物理起源是现代物理学最深远的未解问题之一。虽然宇宙学观测严格约束了状态方程参数w，但仅凭此信息无法揭示暗能量的微观物理，因为许多不同理论模型可以重现相同的膨胀历史。暗能量扰动声速是区分这些模型的关键，但当前天体物理观测对此几乎无法约束。

Method: 构建了一个统一的EFT框架，将动力学暗能量标量场通过对称性驱动的导数相互作用耦合到2HDM+a模型中的赝标量介质子。这些相互作用会诱导不可见衰变并改变BSM介质子在暗能量背景中的传播，导致对撞机上共振性质的 measurable 畸变。

Result: 证明了介质子的衰变宽度、分支比和运动学结构对暗能量涨落的传播性质（尤其是声速）敏感。因此，对撞机观测量为暗能量微观物理提供了直接且互补的探测手段，能够区分在宇宙学上不可区分的模型。

Conclusion: 建立了高能对撞机实验探测宇宙加速物理的新范式，揭示了自然中最小的尺度与最大尺度之间的联系，为揭示暗能量的根本起源开辟了新的实验途径。

Abstract: The physical origin of dark energy remains one of the most profound open questions in modern physics. Although cosmological observations tightly constrain the equation of state parameter $w$, this information alone does not reveal the underlying microphysics, as many distinct theoretical models can reproduce the same expansion history. A key discriminator among these models is the sound speed of dark energy perturbations, yet this quantity remains largely unconstrained by current astrophysical observations. In this work, we propose a fundamentally new approach: using collider measurements of beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) mediator resonances as a probe of dark energy microphysics. We construct a unified effective-field-theory framework in which a dynamical dark energy scalar is coupled, through symmetry-motivated derivative interactions, to a pseudoscalar mediator in the 2HDM+$a$ model. These interactions naturally induce invisible decays and modify the propagation of the BSM mediator in a dark energy background, leading to measurable distortions of resonance properties at colliders such as the LHC. We show that the decay widths, branching ratios, and kinematic structure of the mediator resonance become sensitive to the propagation properties of dark energy fluctuations, in particular the sound speed. As a result, collider observables provide a direct and complementary handle on dark energy microphysics, with the potential to distinguish between models that are otherwise indistinguishable through cosmology alone. Our results establish a new paradigm in which high-energy collider experiments can probe the physics of cosmic acceleration, revealing a connection between the smallest and largest scales in nature and opening a novel experimental pathway to uncover the fundamental origin of dark energy.

### [118] [The one-point charge correlator in deep inelastic scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27454)
*Haotian Cao,Frank Petriello*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Breit框架下提出了深度非弹性散射中单点电荷关联子(QC)的新定义，证明了其红外与共线安全，并利用SCET分别在正向极限和背对背极限下进行了系统分析。正向极限引入核子电荷关联子作为描述核子多维微观结构的新非微扰对象；背对背极限则建立了QC与TMDs的直接对应，实现了标准TMD因子化。奇异性分布已推导至$α_s^2$阶，共线对数实现NLL精度求和，横向动量对数对非极化分布达N$^3$LL精度，对Sivers不对称性达N$^2$LL精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Breit框架下定义单点电荷关联子这一新观测量，并证明其IRC安全性，从而为研究核子微观结构提供新的非微扰探针和理论工具。

Method: 利用SCET分别在正向极限和背对背极限下系统分析QC；在正向极限引入核子电荷关联子作为新的非微扰对象；在背对背极限建立QC与TMDs的因子化对应；进行全QCD计算验证至$α_s^2$阶并执行对数重求和。

Result: QC被证明是IRC安全的；正向极限定义了核子电荷关联子；背对背极限建立了与TMDs的直接对应；奇异性分布通过SCET推导并经全QCD计算至$α_s^2$验证；共线对数实现NLL精度求和，横向动量对数对非极化分布达N$^3$LL，对Sivers不对称性达N$^2$LL精度。

Conclusion: QC是一种IRC安全的可观测量，在正向极限和背对背极限下分别与核子电荷关联子和TMDs相联系，提供了研究核子微观结构的新途径，且高阶求和达到了较高的微扰精度。

Abstract: In this work, we propose a novel definition of the one-point charge correlator (QC) adapted to the Breit frame in deep-inelastic scattering (DIS). We demonstrate that this observable is infrared and collinear (IRC) safe, ensuring its perturbative calculability. Utilizing soft-collinear effective theory (SCET), we systematically analyze the QC in both the forward and back-to-back limits. In the forward limit, we introduce the nucleon charge correlator as a novel non-perturbative object that encodes the multi-dimensional microscopic structure of the nucleon. In the back-to-back limit, the QC establishes a direct correspondence with transverse momentum-dependent distributions (TMDs), enabling its description within the standard TMD factorization formalism. The singular distributions are derived within SCET and are verified by the full QCD calculations up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$. The corresponding collinear logarithms are resummed to all orders with the accuracy of NLL (${\cal{O}}(α_s^n L^{n-1})$), while the transverse momentum-dependent logarithms are resummed to all orders with the accuracy of $N^3$LL for the unpolarized distribution and N$^2$LL for the Sivers asymmetry.

Abstract: Recent results from the LHC on oxygen-oxygen (O-O) and neon-neon (Ne-Ne) collisions open a new window for investigating the interplay of cold nuclear matter (CNM) and quark-gluon plasma (QGP) effects in small collision systems. Building upon recent theoretical work on particle production dynamics in heavy-ion reactions, we present an updated study of light and heavy hadron modification relative to the proton-proton baseline in these systems for selected centralities. Our analysis combines perturbative QCD and hydrodynamic simulations to quantify initial-state effect, collisional energy loss, and medium-induced radiative corrections. We give theoretical predictions at both midrapidity and forward rapidity that can be confronted with ALICE, ATLAS, CMS, and LHCb measurements. Through comparison to the available data, we discuss the relative importance of CNM and QGP effects in O-O and Ne-Ne systems and the role of the heavy quark mass. Our analysis aims to clarify the onset of collective and deconfined behavior in small systems and to provide new insights into the transport properties of matter. We further argue that investigation of other observable such as energy correlators and quarkonia can lead to a more complete picture of QGP formation in these collisions.

Abstract: We present model calculations to reveal the nature of the newly found $Ω^-(2109)$ by the BESIII Collaboration, and show that the state has a strong correlation with the $\bar K^*(892)Ξ$ system. The mediator mass is fixed to 5 GeV. Signal samples of $pp \rightarrow t\bar{t}Y_i$ ($i = 0, 1$) are generated using a MadGraph5_aMC@NLO simplified DM model. Only dileptonic final states of the $t\bar{t}$ system are considered, and the reconstruction is performed through a kinematic fit without explicitly reconstructing the invisible mediator. All relevant Standard Model backgrounds are included. ### [124] [HydroGrav: Precise hydrodynamics and gravitational waves for cosmological phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27775)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: HydroGrav是一个C++代码，用于构建自相似流体剖面并计算引力波谱，支持从有效势直接导出的精确状态方程以及袋模型和μν（改进袋）简化状态方程。通过对比Z2对称标准模型扩展中的简化与精确状态方程，发现两者在峰值振幅和频谱形状上存在差异，并评估了使用精确状态方程对LISA探测器信噪比的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用C++实现HydroGrav代码，从有效势直接确定精确状态方程，构建自相似流体剖面；集成袋模型和μν（改进袋）简化状态方程作为对比；基于声壳模型计算引力波谱；以Z2对称标准模型扩展为例，在参数空间进行扫描，比较简化与精确状态方程在流体剖面、引力波峰值振幅和频谱形状上的差异，并估算对LISA任务信噪比的影响。

Abstract: We present HydroGrav, a C++ code used to construct self-similar fluid profiles, using the exact equation of state determined directly from the effective potential, for any particle physics model capable of producing a first-order electroweak phase transition. HydroGrav also supports the bag and $μν$ (or improved bag) equations of state and includes an implementation of the sound shell model for computing the corresponding gravitational wave spectra. Using this framework, we compare the fluid profiles and gravitational wave spectra for the simplified (bag and $μν$) and exact equations of state for a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric extension of the Standard Model. Furthermore, we perform a scan across the parameter space of this model to identify regions where the simplified and exact equations of state differ in peak amplitude and spectral shape. Finally, we estimate the effect of using the exact equation of state on the signal-to-noise ratio across the parameter space, as measured by LISA after a 4-year mission.

### [125] [Bootstrapping two-loop six-gluon amplitudes in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27801)

Motivation: 将Lipatov等人提出的"QCD振幅中最复杂的项最接近最大超对称Yang-Mills理论"这一观察转化为实用的计算工具，从而系统地计算平面QCD振幅中的最大超越项。

Method: (1) 利用四维主导奇点对有理预因子进行分类和评估，采用壳上图方法；(2) 结合两圈六粒子函数空间，建立符号自举框架；(3) 通过物理一致性条件唯一确定振幅的符号。

Result: 首次确定了平面两圈六胶子振幅在最大权重下的符号，仅需要137个符号字母，并得到了之前未知的两圈三重共线分裂函数和双软分裂函数。

Conclusion: 该方法为QCD振幅中最大超越项的计算提供了实用工具，所得结果具有唯一性和物理一致性，并为进一步研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: The maximally transcendental, or most complicated, terms of gauge-theory scattering amplitudes have long been singled out, following Lipatov and collaborators, as those parts of a QCD amplitude that most closely mirror maximally supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory. We report on a programme that turns this observation into a practical computational tool. We show that the rational prefactors multiplying the highest-weight special functions of planar QCD amplitudes are governed by four-dimensional leading singularities, which can be classified and evaluated using on-shell diagrams. The resulting prefactors are manifestly conformally invariant and admit compact spinor-helicity expressions that hold for arbitrary multiplicity. Combining this input with the recently established two-loop six-particle function space, we set up a symbol bootstrap and determine, for the first time, the maximal-weight symbol of the planar two-loop six-gluon amplitude in massless QCD, first for the ${-}{-}{+}{+}{+}{+}$ helicity configuration and subsequently for all MHV configurations. The answer is fixed uniquely by physical consistency conditions, requires a reduced alphabet of only $137$ symbol letters, and yields as a byproduct previously unknown two-loop triple-collinear and double-soft splitting functions. We summarise the method and the results, and outline the directions they open up.

</details>

Main category: hep-ph

Conclusion: 八元数框架中夸克CP破坏相位被严格局域化为单一参数，轻子CP相位不来自自同构或标准转子，仅可能来自恒等线与轻子-味平面的混合。该结果独立于更广泛的八元数统一纲领，为该框架下的CKM矩阵和PMNS矩阵的完整推导提供了严格的代数约束。

Abstract: One generation of standard-model fermions can be realized on the complexified octonions through the Clifford algebra $\mathcal{C}l(6)$; the octonionic unification programme extends this to three generations, with generation transport implemented by $G_2$ automorphisms or by rotors built from the ladder operators. We prove a localization theorem for the CP-violating phases of this structure, using only the $\mathcal{C}l(6)$ construction and the stated three-generation representatives, independently of the wider programme. For quarks, the first-to-second generation step is the occupation flip of one ladder mode, with the up and down species coupling to conjugate ladder directions; a conjugation theorem forces $A_d=A_u^*$ for every real transport, and the most general rung-generated rotor yields the exact one-parameter law $φ_{12}=-2χ$: the $(1,2)$ transport phase is twice one Yukawa orientation angle. The programme's geometric rotor sits exactly at the quadrature-balanced point $|φ_{12}|=π/2$; the companion analysis reproduces the Cabibbo \emph{magnitude} $|V_{us}|$ with a single real tilt, leaving the rung near quadrature, but it does not extract a CKM CP phase, so the quark Dirac phase is fixed only once the underlying Yukawa orientation is computed. For leptons we prove a reality theorem: every charged-lepton and every neutrino transport amplitude is exactly real for every $G_2$ automorphism and every rotor that does not mix the identity line $\mathbb C\cdot1$ with the lepton--flavor plane $\mathrm{span}(e_7,e_5,e_2)$ a class that contains the entire quark-rung family--and identity--flavor mixing across that plane is the unique possible source of a leptonic phase.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用 PYTHIA 模拟 beauty-hadron 衰变，采用三种强子化场景和真实输入运动学；反氘核形成基于量子力学 coalescence 方法，其波函数来源于 Argonne $v_{18}$ 核子-核子势。

Conclusion: 该研究为 beauty-hadron 衰变产生反氘核提供了定量基准，建立了支持未来实验搜寻的唯象框架，并具有超越对撞机物理的潜在影响（如暗物质间接探测）。

Abstract: Light antinuclei, such as antideuteron ($\bar{\mathrm{d}}$) and antihelium (${}^{3}\overline{\mathrm{He}}$,${}^{4}\overline{\mathrm{He}}$), provide a link between collider physics and indirect Dark Matter searches. Despite extensive studies of antinucleus production in high-energy collisions, $\overline{\mathrm{d}}$ production from beauty-hadron decays remains experimentally unconstrained and has not yet been quantitatively predicted. In this work, we present the first phenomenological study of $\overline{\mathrm{d}}$ production from $\overlineΛ_{b}$ baryon and B$^{-}$ meson decays, providing the first estimates of the corresponding branching ratios. Beauty-hadron decays are simulated with PYTHIA using realistic input kinematics and three hadronization scenarios. Antideuteron formation is modelled through a quantum-mechanical coalescence approach based on an $\bar{\mathrm{d}}$ wave function derived from the Argonne $v_{18}$ nucleon-nucleon potential. The predicted rapidity- and transverse-momentum-differential yields populate the kinematic region where $\overline{\mathrm{d}}$ can be identified by the ALICE experiment, motivating dedicated searches for these decay channels. These results provide a quantitative benchmark for $\overline{\mathrm{d}}$ production from beauty-hadron decays and establish a phenomenological framework to support future experimental searches, with potential implications beyond collider physics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 系统比较了MFIR和MSS两种正则化方案：MFIR将发散真空贡献从有限的磁场依赖项中分离；MSS将这种分离扩展到介质部分，确保仅真空量被正则化。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive review of regularization schemes for magnetized dense quark matter within effective models of quantum chromodynamics, focusing on the Magnetic-Field-Independent Regularization (MFIR) and the Medium Separation Scheme (MSS) at finite chemical potential and magnetic field. In nonrenormalizable frameworks such as the Nambu-Jona-Lasinio model, the treatment of ultraviolet divergences is crucial, particularly in magnetized and dense environments where conventional regularization procedures may introduce unphysical artifacts. We show that MFIR consistently isolates divergent vacuum contributions from finite magnetic-field-dependent terms, while MSS extends this separation to the medium sector, ensuring that only vacuum quantities are regularized. Within this unified framework, we analyze the thermodynamics of cold and dense quark matter, including color-superconducting phases, and demonstrate that the superconducting gap remains finite at large chemical potentials, even in the presence of strong magnetic fields. In contrast to results obtained with traditional regularization schemes, we find no evidence for a transition to a normal phase at zero temperature, highlighting the importance of a proper separation between vacuum and medium contributions. These results eliminate spurious oscillations and other nonphysical artifacts, leading to a more robust and physically consistent description of strongly interacting matter under extreme conditions relevant to compact stars and heavy-ion collisions.

*Pietro Ghedini,Riccardo Impavido,Stefano Gariazzo,Olga Mena,Deng Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用宇宙微波背景辐射（Planck、SPT、ACT）和重子声学振荡（DESI）数据，结合大爆炸核合成（BBN）观测，计算了电子中微子简并参数ξ_{ν_e}和其他中微子种类简并参数ξ_{ν_x}的最新上限。研究考虑了恒定参数和红移依赖（基于PCHIP插值）两种情况，以及三种中微子简并和非简并两种场景。结果表明，BBN数据主要通过影响中子-质子转化率来约束ξ_{ν_e}，在非简并情况下观测到在95%置信水平下偏好非零正值，同时允许更大的哈勃常数H_0。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子中微子简并参数ξ_{ν_e}受BBN严格约束，而其他中微子种类ξ_{ν_x}仅受宇宙学观测弱约束，需要计算最新上限并探索红移依赖的可能性。

Method: 采用PCHIP形式主义构建四个红移节点（z≈10,100,1000,10^8）进行模型无关重构；考虑中微子简并与非简并两种场景；联合CMB（Planck、SPT、ACT）、BAO（DESI）以及BBN观测数据（EMPRESS和LBT）进行宇宙学分析。

Result: BBN数据主要通过中子-质子转化率约束ξ_{ν_e}；在非简并中微子情况下，BBN时期在95%置信水平下偏好非零正值；允许更大的哈勃常数H_0。

Conclusion: 中微子简并参数模型允许更大的H_0，是检验非标准物理模型的有前景场景。

Abstract: The electron neutrino degeneracy parameter, $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{e}} = μ_{ν_\mathrm{e}} / T$, is tightly constrained by Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN), while the degeneracy parameters of the other neutrino species, $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{x}}$, remain weakly constrained by cosmological observations alone. In this manuscript we shall compute up-to-date bounds on $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{e}}$ and $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{x}}$ assuming that either they are constant free-parameters along the cosmic history or that they are redshift dependent quantities. In the latter case we employ a model-independent reconstruction approach based on the Piecewise Cubic Hermite Interpolating Polynomial (PCHIP) formalism with four nodes, located at $z\simeq$ 10, 100, 1000 and $10^8$. We shall also consider two scenarios for neutrinos, specifically three degenerate neutrinos ($ξ_{ν_\mathrm{e}}$ = $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{x}}$) and the case in which we actually differentiate between $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{e}}$ and $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{x}}$. We perform a cosmological analysis combining CMB data from Planck, SPT, and ACT with BAO measurements from DESI, showing the impact of including BBN observables from either EMPRESS results, which allow for a non-zero chemical potential, or from LBT observations, compatible with the standard $ξ_ν$ = 0 prediction. We explicitly show that the BBN data, via the change in neutron-to-proton interconversion rates, mostly constrain $ξ_{ν_\mathrm{e}}$, parameter for which we observe a preferred non-zero positive value at $95\%$ C.L. in the non-degenerate neutrino case at the BBN period. Since the Hubble constant is correlated with $ξ_ν$, through $N_{\rm eff}$, a larger value of $H_0$ is allowed within these models, making them really interesting scenarios where to test non-standard physics models.

</details>


### [134] [Pion and Kaon PDFs via Infrared-Safe Evolution augmented by $J/ψ$ Data Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28168)
*Yanbing Cai,Chengdong Han,Xurong Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在动力部分子模型结合最大熵方法框架下，利用红外安全的QCD演化方案并引入π/K介子诱导的J/ψ强产生数据，对π介子和K介子的部分子分布函数(PDFs)进行了改进测定，显著约束了中、大x区域的胶子分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: π介子和K介子的部分子分布函数(PDFs)由于缺乏高精度实验数据（尤其是胶子分布）而受到很大限制，需要改进测定以更好地理解其非微扰QCD结构。

Method: 采用动力部分子模型结合最大熵方法(MEM)框架，使用红外安全的QCD演化方案使演化可可靠延伸至低Q²（接近强子标度），并在全局拟合中引入π和K介子诱导的J/ψ强产生数据作为关键约束。

Result: 该方法能够很好地描述现有Drell-Yan数据、深度非弹性散射结构函数(F₂)以及不同能量和靶核下的J/ψ产生数据，显著改进了π介子和K介子在中等和大x区域的胶子分布约束。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种更完整的π介子和K介子内部结构图像，特别是在胶子分布方面获得了前所未有的约束。

Abstract: Probing the partonic structure of the pion and the kaon provides essential insights into the non-perturbative dynamics of QCD, yet their parton distribution functions (PDFs) remain poorly constrained due to the scarcity of high-precision experimental data, especially for the gluon distributions. We present an improved determination of pion and kaon PDFs within the dynamical parton model combined with the maximum entropy method (MEM) framework. Our analysis features two key advancements: firstly, we employ an infrared-safe QCD evolution scheme, allowing the evolution to be reliably extended down to very low $Q^2$, approaching the hadronic scale; secondly, we incorporate pion- and kaon-induced $J/ψ$ hadroproduction data as crucial constraints in the global fit. We find that our approach yields a good description of the available Drell-Yan data, deep-inelastic scattering structure functions ($F_2$), and $J/ψ$ production across various energies and targets. The results provide significantly improved constraints on the gluon distributions at moderate and large $x$ in both the pion and the kaon, offering a more complete picture of their internal structure.

### [135] [Real poles with opposite-sign residues in the non-perturbative quark propagator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28212)
*R. Alkofer,M. N. Ferreira,A. S. Miramontes,J. M. Morgado,J. Papavassiliou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 通过完整顶点基函数动态耦合Dyson-Schwinger方程，发现夸克传播子在类时动量区域存在一对实轴极点（而非复数共轭极点），该结构由三个主导顶点形式因子（树图项、反常色磁矩、自旋-动量曲率）共同稳定，产生350 MeV组分夸克质量且保持禁闭特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清夸克传播子在亚GeV类时动量区域的解析结构，解决广泛使用的近似（如彩虹近似）产生复数共轭极点所导致的概念缺陷，同时保持与色禁闭相关的手征对称性破缺和正定性违反的一致性。

Method: 将标准Dyson-Schwinger间隙方程与非微扰夸克-胶子顶点动态耦合，采用完整顶点基函数（12个形式因子），通过逐步调节树图项、反常色磁矩、自旋-动量曲率这三个主导形式因子的强度，系统分析传播子极点行为。

Result: 亚GeV类时动量下传播子存在一对实轴极点（符号相反残差），未出现复数共轭极点；三个主导形式因子的联合作用将极点稳定在实轴上，产生350 MeV组分夸克质量；该结构满足正定性违反（禁闭特征）但规避复数极点带来的理论不一致性。

Conclusion: 完整动力学耦合揭示了夸克传播子解析结构的普适特征：实轴极点结构是量子色动力学非微扰效应的必然结果，而非人为近似引入的赝象；该发现为理解夸克禁闭机制和手征对称性自发破缺提供了新的理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate the analytic structure of the quark propagator in the Landau gauge by dynamically coupling the standard gap equation to the non-perturbative quark-gluon vertex. Employing the full vertex basis, we demonstrate that for sub-GeV time-like momenta, the proper inclusion of the underlying dynamics leads to a pair of real poles with opposite-sign residues. In particular, in stark contradistinction to the results obtained in widely used approximations, we see no sign of complex conjugate poles. This distinctive analytic structure evades conceptual shortcomings frequently associated with complex conjugate poles while remaining fully compatible with the aspects of color confinement related to positivity violation. Crucially, this novel behavior is governed by a dominant triplet of vertex form factors: the tree-level component, the anomalous chromomagnetic moment, and a component we label as "spin-momentum curvature". By gradually tuning the individual strengths of these components, we demonstrate that while they contribute in distinct ways to the quark propagator, their joint action is vital for stabilizing the system. Together, they place the low-lying poles onto the real axis while producing a robust constituent quark mass of $350$ MeV.

</details>


### [136] [Neural-Network extraction of TMDs with SIDIS data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28218)
*Matteo Cerutti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次基于神经网络参数化对非极化横向动量依赖（TMD）分布进行全局分析，同时纳入Drell-Yan（DY）和半单举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）数据，精度达到N³LL。结果表明，SIDIS数据的加入使得非极化TMD PDF比仅用DY的神经网络提取更宽，不确定性相比仅DY情形有所减少，但仍大于传统模型的结果。该工作展示了灵活神经网络参数化在降低模型依赖性方面的潜力，并为未来Jefferson Lab和电子-离子对撞机的高精度测量提供指导。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用神经网络参数化非极化TMD分布，同时拟合Drell-Yan和半单举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）数据，在N³LL精度下进行全局分析，并与仅使用DY数据的神经网络提取及传统模型结果进行比较。

Result: 同时包含SIDIS和DY数据的神经网络提取得到的非极化TMD PDF比仅DY的神经网络提取更宽；不确定性相比仅DY情形降低，但仍大于传统模型方法得到的不确定性。

Conclusion: 灵活的神经网络参数化能有效降低TMD提取中的模型依赖性，SIDIS数据对非极化TMD PDF提供了额外约束；该工作为未来Jefferson Lab和EIC的高精度测量提供了参考基准。

Abstract: A first global analysis of unpolarized Transverse-Momentum-Dependent (TMD) distributions based on a neural-network (NN) parametrization is presented. Drell-Yan (DY) and semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering (SIDIS) data are simultaneously included at next-to-next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic (N$^3$LL) accuracy. The results indicate that the inclusion of SIDIS data leads to broader unpolarized TMD PDFs compared to a DY-only NN extraction. The associated uncertainties are reduced with respect to the DY-only case, while remaining larger than the ones obtained using traditional models. These results demonstrate the potential of flexible NN parametrizations in reducing model dependence and provide guidance for future high-precision measurements at Jefferson Lab and the Electron-Ion Collider.
