### [137] [Neutrino oscillation data and a pseudo-Dirac heavy neutral lepton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28272)
*Jan Hajer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了对称性保护的跷跷板模型，其中轻中微子质量的小量性由近似的轻子数对称性保护，仅被小参数破坏。在最小场景中（一个伪狄拉克HNL对），通过精确对角化狄拉克极限并结合微扰处理轻子数破坏项，重建了活性-重子相互作用矩阵。秩二轻中微子质量矩阵固定了归一化活性味方向，而高能信息简化为一个复振幅及其CP奇性不变式。归一化活性-重子相互作用权重中，振幅与重子区旋转抵消，在味单纯形中留下由振荡数据和马约拉纳相位决定的椭圆。同时识别了线性轻子数破坏项如何影响相干重中微子振荡和无中微子双贝塔有效质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在对称性保护的跷跷板模型中，轻中微子质量的小量性由近似的轻子数对称性保护，使得重中性轻子能够在LHC对撞机可及范围内。然而，活性-重子混合矩阵的味结构尚未被充分解析，特别是如何从低能中微子振荡数据重建高能参数空间，以及CP破坏相位的物理效应尚不清晰。

Method: 采用非微扰精确对角化处理轻子数守恒的狄拉克极限，然后对小的轻子数破坏项进行微扰展开。通过秩二轻中微子质量矩阵约束活性味方向，将高能自由参数简化为单个复振幅，并构造CP奇性轻-重不变式。利用归一化权重消除重子区旋转自由度，在味单纯形中导出椭圆参数化。

Result: 成功重建了对称性保护下的活性-重子相互作用矩阵的味结构。归一化活性-重子相互作用权重与高能复振幅和重子区旋转无关，仅由轻中微子振荡数据和马约拉纳相位决定，在味单纯形中表现为椭圆。线性轻子数破坏项在相干重中微子振荡和无中微子双贝塔衰变中产生可观测效应。

Conclusion: 对称性保护的跷跷板模型具有高度可预测的味结构，低能中微子数据能够高精度约束高能参数空间。归一化活性-重子相互作用权重的椭圆参数化提供了模型无关的检验窗口，而CP破坏相位可通过重中微子振荡和0νββ衰变进行实验探测。

Abstract: Symmetry-protected seesaw models can accommodate light-neutrino oscillation data while keeping heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) within collider reach. In these models, the smallness of the light-neutrino masses is protected by an approximate lepton number (LN)-like symmetry that is broken only by small parameters. We study the minimal scenario in which the new states form one pseudo-Dirac HNL pair. The exact LN-conserving Dirac limit is diagonalised without expanding in the active-sterile mixing, and the small LN-violating entries are then included perturbatively. This yields a symmetry-protected flavour reconstruction of the active-heavy interaction matrix. The rank-two light-neutrino mass matrix fixes the normalised active-flavour direction, while the remaining high-energy information is a single complex light-heavy amplitude whose phase defines a CP-odd light-heavy invariant. For the normalised leading active-heavy interaction weights, this amplitude and the heavy-sector rotation cancel, leaving an ellipse in the flavour simplex determined by light-neutrino oscillation data and the Majorana phase. We also identify how the linear LN-violating terms enter coherent heavy-neutrino oscillations and the neutrinoless double beta effective mass.

### [138] [Revealing precision bounds on neutrino oscillation parameters with quantum estimation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28275)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应用量子估计理论框架到中微子振荡中，澄清基矢选择等微妙问题，揭示振荡参数的最大可实现精度。

Method: 以两味振荡为例分析基矢变换对QFI的影响；对三味振荡，在味基下计算电子和中微子态的QFI矩阵，推导对角和非对角元素的解析表达式与数值结果。

Result: 获得了QFI矩阵的解析表达式与数值结果，讨论了非对角相关性对多参数估计的影响，给出了典型反应堆和长基线加速器中微子实验的量子Cramér-Rao下界。

Abstract: Quantum estimation theory provides ultimate precision bounds on parameter estimation, independent of experimental setups. In this article, we apply this theoretical framework to neutrino oscillations, aiming to clarify some subtle issues and reveal the maximum achievable precision of oscillation parameters. First, taking the example of two-flavor oscillations, we clarify how the quantum Fisher information (QFI) depends on the choice of bases when the basis transformation itself involves the parameters in question. Then, for three-flavor oscillations, we compute the QFI matrix for electron and muon neutrino states in the flavor basis and derive analytical expressions and numerical results for both diagonal and off-diagonal elements. The implications of off-diagonal correlations for multiparameter estimation are discussed, and the quantum Cramér-Rao bounds on the precision of oscillation parameters for typical reactor and long-baseline accelerator neutrino experiments are obtained. Our results establish a theoretical benchmark for the ultimate precision achievable in future neutrino oscillation experiments.

### [139] [Particle Production from Inhomogeneities: the off-shell side of gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28297)
*Michele Redi,Andrea Tesi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了早期宇宙中由引力不均匀性产生的粒子生产，推导了粒子产量与应力-能量张量两点函数之间的普遍关系，建立了暗物质生产与引力波信号之间的现象学联系，并指出在亚视界尺度上粒子生产实际上简化为引力散射，最后将该形式应用于一级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究早期宇宙中来自引力不均匀性的粒子生产，特别是建立暗物质生产与引力波信号之间的现象学联系，从而通过引力波背景振幅推断暗物质质量。

Method: 推导了粒子产量与标量、矢量和张量度规扰动的应力-能量张量的不等时两点函数之间的普遍表达式；在亚视界尺度上，证明了粒子生产简化为引力散射，将形式与标准模型热浴的引力冻结机制联系起来，并将其扩展到非热和非平衡源。

Result: 粒子产量探测了应力-能量张量关联函数的时间型支撑；在张量情形下，同一物理量在光锥型支撑上的取值控制引力波发射；粒子生产在亚视界尺度上简化为引力散射；该机制可有效填充引力耦合的暗区，尤其当扰动在暴胀后不久产生时。

Conclusion: 建立了暗物质生产与引力波信号之间的现象学联系，使得暗物质质量与随机引力波背景的振幅可以相关联；将该形式应用于一级相变，并讨论了标量和张量扰动相关的粒子生产。

Abstract: We continue the study of particle production from gravitational inhomogeneities in the early Universe. Focusing on sources active on sub-horizon scales, we derive general expressions relating particle production to the unequal-time two-point function of the stress-energy tensor sourcing scalar, vector and tensor metric perturbations. The resulting particle yield probes the time-like support of this correlator, and in the tensor case the same object controls gravitational wave emission when evaluated on the light-like support. This establishes a phenomenological link between dark matter production and gravitational wave signals, allowing the dark matter mass to be related to the amplitude of the stochastic gravitational wave background. Our results show that, on sub-horizon scales, particle production from inhomogeneous metric backgrounds practically reduces to gravitational scattering. This directly connects the formalism to gravitational freeze-in from the Standard Model thermal bath, while extending it to non-thermal and out of equilibrium sources. We apply the formalism to first order phase transitions and discuss the associated production from scalar and tensor perturbations. The mechanism can efficiently populate gravitationally coupled dark sectors, especially when the perturbations are generated shortly after inflation.

### [140] [Near-threshold scattering of proton and Omega baryon and possible bound states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28319)
*Yu-Jie Feng,Qian Wang,Qiang Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究NΩ系统的近阈值散射和束缚态结构，探究波莫朗交换机制在该系统中的动力学作用。

Method: 在介子交换模型和波莫朗交换模型框架下，通过求解Lippmann-Schwinger (L-S)方程进行数值计算。

Result: 1) 引入波莫朗交换后，⁵S₂通道的束缚能、散射长度和有效范围等可观测量与实验测量更吻合；2) 波莫朗交换提供额外吸引相互作用使强子态更致密；3) 预测³S₁通道存在弱准束缚态。

Conclusion: 波莫朗交换机制在NΩ系统中起重要动力学作用，未来³S₁通道的实验测量将为验证该机制提供关键判据。

Abstract: We study the near-threshold scattering and bound-state structure of the $NΩ$ system by solving the Lippmann-Schwinger (L-S) equation within the framework of the meson exchange model and the Pomeron exchange model. The numerical results indicate that after incorporating the Pomeron exchange mechanism, the observables of the ${^5}S{_2}$ channel, such as the binding energy, scattering length, and effective range, agree better with the experimental measurements. In addition, The Pomeron exchange can provide an extra attractive interaction to make the hadronic state more compact. We also predict the scattering behavior of the ${^3}S{_1}$ channel and confirm that a weak quasi-bound state exists in this channel. Future experimental measurements on the ${^3}S{_1}$ channel will provide an important criterion for verifying the dynamic role played by the Pomeron exchange mechanism within the $NΩ$ system.
